# 3) Connect to Google Sheet + Apps Script (Ops automation)

``/**  * On form submit: post to Discord + email Ops.  * 1) Set your Discord webhook URL  * 2) Set your Ops email  */ const DISCORD_WEBHOOK = 'https://discord.com/api/webhooks/XXXXX/XXXXX'; const OPS_EMAIL = 'ops@yourdomain.tld';  function onFormSubmit(e) {   try {     const headers = e.namedValues; // column header -> array of values     const payload = formatPayload(headers);      // 1) Discord webhook     UrlFetchApp.fetch(DISCORD_WEBHOOK, {       method: 'post',       contentType: 'application/json',       payload: JSON.stringify({         username: 'Vault Ops Bot',         content: `**New Vetting Submission**\n${payload.discord}`       })     });      // 2) Email Ops     MailApp.sendEmail({       to: OPS_EMAIL,       subject: '[VAULT] New Vetting Submission',       htmlBody: payload.html     });    } catch (err) {     console.error(err);     MailApp.sendEmail({       to: OPS_EMAIL,       subject: '[VAULT] Apps Script Error',       htmlBody: `<pre>${sanitize(String(err))}</pre>`     });   } }  function formatPayload(named) {   // Adjust keys to match your Form question titles exactly   const name = first(named['Full name / Alias']);   const email = first(named['Email']);   const city = first(named['Country / City']);   const role = first(named['Role']);   const sources = first(named['Links to credible sources']);   const handle = first(named['Telegram/Signal handle']);   const langs = first(named['Languages']);    const discord =     `Name/Alias: ${name}\n` +     `Email: ${email}\n` +     `Location: ${city}\n` +     `Role: ${role}\n` +     `Sources:\n${sources}\n` +     (handle ? `Handle: ${handle}\n` : '') +     (langs ? `Languages: ${langs}\n` : '');    const html =     `<b>Name/Alias:</b> ${esc(name)}<br>` +     `<b>Email:</b> ${esc(email)}<br>` +     `<b>Location:</b> ${esc(city)}<br>` +     `<b>Role:</b> ${esc(role)}<br>` +     `<b>Sources:</b><br><pre>${esc(sources)}</pre>` +     (handle ? `<b>Handle:</b> ${esc(handle)}<br>` : '') +     (langs ? `<b>Languages:</b> ${esc(langs)}<br>` : '');    return { discord, html }; }  function first(arr) { return Array.isArray(arr) ? (arr[0] || '') : (arr || ''); } function esc(s) { return String(s).replace(/[&<>]/g, m => ({'&':'&amp;','<':'&lt;','>':'&gt;'}[m])); } function sanitize(s){ return esc(s).slice(0, 5000); }``

**Triggers:**Â Apps Script â†’ Triggers â†’ â€œ+ Add Triggerâ€

- Function:Â `onFormSubmit`
    
- Event source: â€œFrom spreadsheetâ€

Hereâ€™s whatâ€™s most likely going on and why youâ€™re seeing itÂ _now_Â even though you never had to before:

---

## **Why Itâ€™s Happening**

1. **IP Reputation Change**
    
    - If youâ€™re on ProtonVPN or another VPN, Cloudflare sees aÂ _shared_Â IP with thousands of other users.
        
    - If a few of those users trigger security filters on OpenAIâ€™s edge network,Â _everyone_Â on that IP gets challenged.
        
2. **Frequent IP Switching**
    
    - VPN auto-reconnect or unstable Wi-Fi can cause your IP to change mid-session. Cloudflare sees you as a â€œnewâ€ visitor each time â†’ forces another check.
        
3. **Browser Cache or Token Timeout**
    
    - If your browser wipes cookies or blocks certain scripts, your session tokens canâ€™t persist â†’ you keep getting kicked back to the login screen.
        
4. **Security Settings Just Got Stricter**
    
    - OpenAI (or their Cloudflare config) mightâ€™ve tightened anti-bot checks recently â€” meaning sessions now get challenged more aggressively.
        

---

## **How to Stop It**

### **Option A â€” Stick to a Stable, Trusted IP**

- If youâ€™re on a VPN, switch to a server withÂ _low load_Â and ideally in the same region you normally use ChatGPT from.
    
- If you trust your network, temporarily tryÂ **without VPN**Â and see if the looping stops.
    
- If it does, itâ€™s definitely VPN IP reputation.
    

### **Option B â€” Keep Session Tokens Alive**

- Donâ€™t close the tab â€” leave ChatGPT open in one pinned tab.
    
- Make sure your browser isnâ€™t set to auto-clear cookies/cache when closing.
    
- In Chrome: Settings â†’ Privacy & Security â†’ Site settings â†’ Cookies â†’ Allow for chat.openai.com.
    

### **Option C â€” Reduce Browser Conflicts**

- Disable privacy extensions that block JavaScript, cookies, or inject headers (uBlock, Privacy Badger, etc.) forÂ `chat.openai.com`.

## 3) Reset the working tree to the backup (no .git contamination)

Weâ€™ll replace the repo contents with your backup, butÂ **preserve**Â theÂ `.git`Â directory so the remote stays wired.

`cd ~/Documents/papiricanpi.github.io || mkdir -p ~/Documents/papiricanpi.github.io && cd ~/Documents/papiricanpi.github.io  # kill any half-done rebase/merge git rebase --abort 2>/dev/null || true git merge --abort 2>/dev/null || true  # hard-clean the repo (except .git) find . -mindepth 1 -maxdepth 1 ! -name ".git" -exec rm -rf {} +  # copy backup contents in (excluding any stray .git from backup) rsync -a --delete --exclude='.git' ~/Documents/VAULT_RESTORE/ ./`

> IfÂ `rsync`Â complains on macOS, runÂ `brew install rsync`Â or replace withÂ `cp -a ~/Documents/VAULT_RESTORE/. ./`

# Common â€œgotchaâ€ fixes (rapid-fire)

- **fatal: not a git repository**  
    â†’ Youâ€™re in the wrong folder.Â `cd ~/Documents/papiricanpi.github.io`Â thenÂ `git init && git branch -M main && git remote add origin <URL>`.
    
- **â€œinteractive rebase in progressâ€**  
    â†’Â `git rebase --abort`Â then continue.
    
- **Large file rejection (LFS)**  
    â†’ Remove giant binaries from the repo or wire up Git LFS; for GH Pages, avoid >100MB files.
    
- **Permission denied on scripts**  
    â†’Â `chmod +x scripts/*.sh`Â if you have deploy helpers (not required for Pages).
    
- **Pages builds but CSS/JS broken**  
    â†’ Check paths. UseÂ **relative paths**Â (`/assets/...`Â from root, orÂ `./assets/...`Â if needed). Donâ€™t rely onÂ `baseurl`Â unless you set it.

That error means your script has a bare wordÂ **`Drop`**Â on line 10 â€” JavaScript thinks itâ€™s a variable but itâ€™s not defined, so it fails.

It usually happens if you pasted a CSV value or label directly into code without quotes.  
For example:

âŒ Wrong:

`if (status === Drop) { ... }`

âœ… Correct:

`if (status === "Drop") { ... }`

---

### How to fix:

1. **Open**Â your Apps Script (`Code.gs`).
    
2. **Go to line 10**Â where it saysÂ `Drop`Â without quotes.
    
3. Wrap it in quotes if itâ€™s meant to be a string:
    
    `if (status === "Drop") { ... }`
    
4. If it was supposed to be a variable name, make sure itâ€™s declared:
    
    `const Drop = "Drop";`
    
    But in our evidence triage script, itâ€™s always meant to be a string.

###### ChatGPT said:

---

### Why this matters

When you wroteÂ `Drop`Â without quotes, Google Apps Script thought you were referring to a variable namedÂ `Drop`Â that doesnâ€™t exist. Wrapping it in quotes tells the interpreter itâ€™s just a text value to compare against.

Hereâ€™s aÂ **clean, plug-and-play Google Apps Script**Â for yourÂ **Evidence Drop**Â sheet â€” includes theÂ `"Drop"`Â status handling, auto-stamp dates, severity suggestions,Â **Discord ping**Â (for High only), andÂ **Ops email**. ### 1) Paste this into your Sheetâ€™s Script Editor (replace everything)

``/***** VAULT â€” Evidence Drop Automation (paste in Code.gs) *****  * What it does:  * - Auto-stamp "Reviewed Date" when "Triage Status" changes  * - Suggest "Severity" from Links+Description keywords  * - Normalize "Links to Evidence" to https://.. if missing  * - Ping Discord + email Ops when Severity is "High"  * - Handle explicit status === "Drop" safely  **************************************************************/  /** CONFIG â€” EDIT THESE TWO */ const DISCORD_WEBHOOK = "PASTE_YOUR_OPS_ALERTS_WEBHOOK";   // e.g., https://discord.com/api/webhooks/xxx/yyy const OPS_EMAIL       = "your_ops_email@proton.me";  /** OPTIONAL: name of your working sheet (tab). Leave null to use the active sheet */ const SHEET_NAME = null;  /** === MAIN ON-EDIT HOOK (install a trigger: From spreadsheet â†’ On edit) === */ function onEditEvidence(e) {   try {     const sh = SHEET_NAME ? e.source.getSheetByName(SHEET_NAME) : e.range.getSheet();     if (!sh) return;      const header = sh.getRange(1, 1, 1, sh.getLastColumn()).getValues()[0];      // Resolve columns by header text (case-insensitive regex)     const col = {       triage:  findHeader(header, /triage status/i),       reviewed:findHeader(header, /reviewed date/i),       severity:findHeader(header, /severity/i),       who:     findHeader(header, /name of individual\/organization/i),       links:   findHeader(header, /links to evidence/i),       desc:    findHeader(header, /brief description/i),       notes:   findHeader(header, /notes/i)     };      const r = e.range.getRow();     const c = e.range.getColumn();     if (r === 1) return; // ignore header edits      // Stamp Reviewed Date when TRIAGE changes     if (c === col.triage && col.reviewed > 0) {       sh.getRange(r, col.reviewed).setValue(new Date());     }      // Suggest Severity on edits to links/description/triage     if ([col.links, col.desc, col.triage].includes(c) && col.severity > 0) {       const links = getCell(sh, r, col.links);       const desc  = getCell(sh, r, col.desc);       sh.getRange(r, col.severity).setValue(suggestSeverity(`${links} ${desc}`));     }      // Normalize link when Links column edited     if (c === col.links && col.links > 0) {       const v = String(getCell(sh, r, col.links) || "").trim();       if (v && !/^https?:\/\//i.test(v)) sh.getRange(r, col.links).setValue("https://" + v);     }      // Handle explicit Drop status (no syntax errors)     if (col.triage > 0) {       const status = String(getCell(sh, r, col.triage) || "").trim();       if (status === "Drop") {         // Optional: annotate notes, set severity low         if (col.notes > 0) sh.getRange(r, col.notes).setNote("Marked Drop by Ops");         if (col.severity > 0) sh.getRange(r, col.severity).setValue("Low");       }     }      // If severity is HIGH, ping Discord + email Ops (once per edit)     if (col.severity > 0) {       const sev = String(getCell(sh, r, col.severity) || "");       if (sev.toLowerCase() === "high") {         const who   = col.who   > 0 ? String(getCell(sh, r, col.who)   || "") : "";         const links = col.links > 0 ? String(getCell(sh, r, col.links) || "") : "";         const desc  = col.desc  > 0 ? String(getCell(sh, r, col.desc)  || "") : "";          safePingDiscord(`ğŸš¨ **High Severity Evidence** **Name/Org:** ${who} **Links:** ${links} **Notes:** ${desc ? (desc.length>500 ? desc.slice(0,500)+'â€¦' : desc) : '(none)'} (Row ${r})`);          safeMail(OPS_EMAIL, "[VAULT] High Severity Evidence", htmlPre(` High Severity Evidence (Row ${r})  Name/Org: ${who} Links:    ${links} Notes:    ${desc} `));       }     }    } catch (err) {     Logger.log("onEditEvidence error: " + err);   } }  /** === UTILITIES === */ function findHeader(headerRow, regex) {   for (var i = 0; i < headerRow.length; i++) {     var h = String(headerRow[i] || "");     if (regex.test(h)) return i + 1; // 1-based col index   }   return -1; } function getCell(sh, row, col) { return (col > 0) ? sh.getRange(row, col).getValue() : ""; }  function suggestSeverity(text) {   const t = String(text || "").toLowerCase();   const high = /(fraud|money laundering|kickback|ghost|scam|theft|embezzl|bribe|pork)/;   const med  = /(nepotism|conflict|misuse|misreport|coi|irregular)/;   if (high.test(t)) return "High";   if (med.test(t))  return "Medium";   return "Low"; }  function safePingDiscord(content) {   try {     if (!DISCORD_WEBHOOK || DISCORD_WEBHOOK.indexOf("https://") !== 0) return;     UrlFetchApp.fetch(DISCORD_WEBHOOK, {       method: "post",       contentType: "application/json",       payload: JSON.stringify({ username: "Vault Evidence Bot", content })     });   } catch (e) { Logger.log("Discord error: " + e); } }  function safeMail(to, subject, htmlBody) {   try {     if (!to) return;     MailApp.sendEmail({ to, subject, htmlBody });   } catch (e) { Logger.log("Mail error: " + e); } }  function htmlPre(text) {   const esc = String(text).replace(/[&<>]/g, m => ({'&':'&amp;','<':'&lt;','>':'&gt;'}[m]));   return "<pre style='font-family:monospace'>" + esc + "</pre>"; }  /** === BULK BACKFILL (menu action) === */ function triageBackfillAll() {   const sh = SHEET_NAME ? SpreadsheetApp.getActive().getSheetByName(SHEET_NAME)                         : SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSheet();   const header = sh.getRange(1, 1, 1, sh.getLastColumn()).getValues()[0];   const col = {     triage:  findHeader(header, /triage status/i),     reviewed:findHeader(header, /reviewed date/i),     severity:findHeader(header, /severity/i),     links:   findHeader(header, /links to evidence/i),     desc:    findHeader(header, /brief description/i)   };   const last = sh.getLastRow();   for (var r = 2; r <= last; r++) {     try {       const triage = String(getCell(sh, r, col.triage) || "");       const reviewed = getCell(sh, r, col.reviewed);       if (triage && triage.toLowerCase() !== "new" && !reviewed && col.reviewed > 0) {         sh.getRange(r, col.reviewed).setValue(new Date());       }       if (col.severity > 0) {         const links = String(getCell(sh, r, col.links) || "");         const desc  = String(getCell(sh, r, col.desc)  || "");         sh.getRange(r, col.severity).setValue(suggestSeverity(`${links} ${desc}`));       }     } catch (_) {}   } }  /** Add menu for backfill */ function onOpen() {   SpreadsheetApp.getUi()     .createMenu("Vault Ops")     .addItem("Backfill Triage/Severity", "triageBackfillAll")     .addToUi(); }``

Apps Script editor â†’Â **Triggers (â°)**Â â†’Â **Add Trigger**

- Function:Â `onEditEvidence`
    
- Event source:Â **From spreadsheet**
    
- Event type:Â **On edit**

### 3) Wire your webhook + email

    - `PASTE_YOUR_OPS_ALERTS_WEBHOOK`Â â†’ yourÂ **#ops-alerts**Â Discord webhook

``// === CONFIG === const DISCORD_WEBHOOK = "PASTE_YOUR_OPS_ALERTS_WEBHOOK";  // Your #ops-alerts webhook const OPS_EMAIL = "your_ops_email@proton.me";              // Your Proton inbox  // === MAIN TRIGGER FUNCTION === function onEditEvidence(e) {   const sh = e.range.getSheet();   const headerRow = 1;   const statusColName = "Status"; // Must match the header in your sheet    const row = e.range.getRow();   if (row <= headerRow) return;    const dataRange = sh.getRange(headerRow, 1, 1, sh.getLastColumn());   const headers = dataRange.getValues()[0];   const statusCol = headers.indexOf(statusColName) + 1;   if (statusCol < 1) return;    const status = sh.getRange(row, statusCol).getValue();   if (status === "Drop") {     const rowData = sh.getRange(row, 1, 1, sh.getLastColumn()).getValues()[0];     const payload = formatPayload(headers, rowData);      sendDiscordAlert(payload);     sendEmailAlert(payload);   } }  // === HELPERS === function formatPayload(headers, rowData) {   let msg = "**ğŸš¨ Evidence Drop Alert ğŸš¨**\n";   for (let i = 0; i < headers.length; i++) {     msg += `**${headers[i]}:** ${rowData[i]}\n`;   }   return msg; }  function sendDiscordAlert(message) {   const payload = JSON.stringify({ content: message });   UrlFetchApp.fetch(DISCORD_WEBHOOK, {     method: "post",     contentType: "application/json",     payload: payload   }); }  function sendEmailAlert(message) {   MailApp.sendEmail({     to: OPS_EMAIL,     subject: "ğŸš¨ Evidence Drop Alert",     body: message   }); }``

## Fix in 30 seconds

1. In the Apps Script editor, click in the code pane and pressÂ **Cmd-A**Â (Ctrl-A on Windows) toÂ **select everything**.
    
2. PressÂ **Delete**Â so the file is completely empty.
    
3. Paste thisÂ **entire**Â clean file (it replaces everything):
    

``/***** VAULT â€” Evidence Drop Automation (single-file, paste all of this) *****/  // === CONFIG (EDIT THESE) === const DISCORD_WEBHOOK = "PASTE_YOUR_OPS_ALERTS_WEBHOOK";   // e.g., https://discord.com/api/webhooks/xxx/yyy const OPS_EMAIL       = "your_ops_email@proton.me";        // your inbox  // === MAIN ON-EDIT TRIGGER === function onEditEvidence(e) {   try {     const sh = e.range.getSheet();     const header = sh.getRange(1, 1, 1, sh.getLastColumn()).getValues()[0];      // Resolve columns by header text (adjust if your headers differ)     const col = {       status:  findHeader(header, /status|triage status/i),       reviewed:findHeader(header, /reviewed date/i),       severity:findHeader(header, /severity/i),       who:     findHeader(header, /name of individual\/organization/i),       links:   findHeader(header, /links to evidence/i),       desc:    findHeader(header, /brief description/i),       notes:   findHeader(header, /notes/i),     };      const r = e.range.getRow(), c = e.range.getColumn();     if (r === 1) return; // ignore header      // Stamp Reviewed Date when Status/Triage edits     if (c === col.status && col.reviewed > 0) {       sh.getRange(r, col.reviewed).setValue(new Date());     }      // Suggest severity on edits to links/description/status     if ([col.links, col.desc, col.status].includes(c) && col.severity > 0) {       const links = getCell(sh, r, col.links);       const desc  = getCell(sh, r, col.desc);       sh.getRange(r, col.severity).setValue(suggestSeverity(`${links} ${desc}`));     }      // Normalize links when edited     if (c === col.links && col.links > 0) {       const v = String(getCell(sh, r, col.links) || "").trim();       if (v && !/^https?:\/\//i.test(v)) sh.getRange(r, col.links).setValue("https://" + v);     }      // Handle explicit Drop     if (col.status > 0) {       const status = String(getCell(sh, r, col.status) || "").trim();       if (status === "Drop") {         if (col.notes > 0) sh.getRange(r, col.notes).setNote("Marked Drop by Ops");         if (col.severity > 0) sh.getRange(r, col.severity).setValue("Low");       }     }      // If severity is High â†’ ping Discord + email Ops     if (col.severity > 0) {       const sev = String(getCell(sh, r, col.severity) || "");       if (sev.toLowerCase() === "high") {         const who   = col.who   > 0 ? String(getCell(sh, r, col.who)   || "") : "";         const links = col.links > 0 ? String(getCell(sh, r, col.links) || "") : "";         const desc  = col.desc  > 0 ? String(getCell(sh, r, col.desc)  || "") : "";          safePingDiscord(`ğŸš¨ **High Severity Evidence** **Name/Org:** ${who} **Links:** ${links} **Notes:** ${desc ? (desc.length>500 ? desc.slice(0,500)+'â€¦' : desc) : '(none)'} (Row ${r})`);          safeMail(OPS_EMAIL, "[VAULT] High Severity Evidence", htmlPre(` High Severity Evidence (Row ${r})  Name/Org: ${who} Links:    ${links} Notes:    ${desc} `));       }     }   } catch (err) {     Logger.log("onEditEvidence error: " + err);   } }  // === UTILITIES === function findHeader(headerRow, regex) {   for (var i = 0; i < headerRow.length; i++) {     var h = String(headerRow[i] || "");     if (regex.test(h)) return i + 1; // 1-based   }   return -1; } function getCell(sh, row, col) { return (col > 0) ? sh.getRange(row, col).getValue() : ""; }  function suggestSeverity(text) {   const t = String(text || "").toLowerCase();   const high = /(fraud|money laundering|kickback|ghost|scam|theft|embezzl|bribe|pork)/;   const med  = /(nepotism|conflict|misuse|misreport|coi|irregular)/;   if (high.test(t)) return "High";   if (med.test(t))  return "Medium";   return "Low"; }  function safePingDiscord(content) {   try {     if (!DISCORD_WEBHOOK || DISCORD_WEBHOOK.indexOf("https://") !== 0) return;     UrlFetchApp.fetch(DISCORD_WEBHOOK, {       method: "post",       contentType: "application/json",       payload: JSON.stringify({ username: "Vault Evidence Bot", content })     });   } catch (e) { Logger.log("Discord error: " + e); } }  function safeMail(to, subject, htmlBody) {   try {     if (!to) return;     MailApp.sendEmail({ to, subject, htmlBody });   } catch (e) { Logger.log("Mail error: " + e); } }  function htmlPre(text) {   const esc = String(text).replace(/[&<>]/g, m => ({'&':'&amp;','<':'&lt;','>':'&gt;'}[m]));   return "<pre style='font-family:monospace'>" + esc + "</pre>"; }  /** Optional: manual backfill via menu */ function triageBackfillAll() {   const sh = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSheet();   const header = sh.getRange(1, 1, 1, sh.getLastColumn()).getValues()[0];   const col = {     status:  findHeader(header, /status|triage status/i),     reviewed:findHeader(header, /reviewed date/i),     severity:findHeader(header, /severity/i),     links:   findHeader(header, /links to evidence/i),     desc:    findHeader(header, /brief description/i),   };   const last = sh.getLastRow();   for (var r = 2; r <= last; r++) {     try {       const status = String(getCell(sh, r, col.status) || "");       const reviewed = getCell(sh, r, col.reviewed);       if (status && status.toLowerCase() !== "new" && !reviewed && col.reviewed > 0) {         sh.getRange(r, col.reviewed).setValue(new Date());       }       if (col.severity > 0) {         const links = String(getCell(sh, r, col.links) || "");         const desc  = String(getCell(sh, r, col.desc)  || "");         sh.getRange(r, col.severity).setValue(suggestSeverity(`${links} ${desc}`));       }     } catch (_) {}   } }  function onOpen() {   SpreadsheetApp.getUi()     .createMenu("Vault Ops")     .addItem("Backfill Triage/Severity", "triageBackfillAll")     .addToUi(); }``

## 2) Paste this script (works with those exact headers)

``/***** VAULT â€” Evidence Drop (Form Responses 1 + Ops columns on the right) *****/  // EDIT THESE const DISCORD_WEBHOOK = "https://discord.com/api/webhooks/XXXXXXXX/XXXXXXXX"; const OPS_EMAIL       = "pimpfiles@proton.me";  // Column names (must match row 1 exactly) const COLS = {   triage:   "Triage Status",   reviewed: "Reviewed Date",   severity: "Severity",   who:      "Name of Individual/Organization",  // if your Form uses a different label, change this   links:    "Share 1â€“3 links that show your signal (thread", // partial match handled below   desc:     "Brief Description",                 // change if your label is different   notes:    "Notes" };  // main trigger function onEditEvidence(e) {   try {     const sh = e && e.range ? e.range.getSheet() : SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSheet();     if (!sh) return;      const header = sh.getRange(1,1,1,sh.getLastColumn()).getValues()[0];      // resolve columns by exact/startsWith match     const col = {       triage:   findCol(header, COLS.triage),       reviewed: findCol(header, COLS.reviewed),       severity: findCol(header, COLS.severity),       who:      findCol(header, COLS.who, true),       links:    findCol(header, COLS.links,  true),  // allow startsWith for long form labels       desc:     findCol(header, COLS.desc,   true),       notes:    findCol(header, COLS.notes)     };      const r = e && e.range ? e.range.getRow() : 2;     const c = e && e.range ? e.range.getColumn() : 1;     if (r === 1) return;      // stamp Reviewed Date when triage changes     if (c === col.triage && col.reviewed > 0) {       sh.getRange(r, col.reviewed).setValue(new Date());     }      // suggest severity on edits to links/desc/triage     if ([col.links, col.desc, col.triage].includes(c) && col.severity > 0) {       const links = get(sh, r, col.links);       const desc  = get(sh, r, col.desc);       sh.getRange(r, col.severity).setValue(suggest(`${links} ${desc}`));     }      // normalize links when edited     if (c === col.links && col.links > 0) {       const v = String(get(sh, r, col.links) || "").trim();       if (v && !/^https?:\/\//i.test(v)) sh.getRange(r, col.links).setValue("https://" + v);     }      // explicit dropped status     if (col.triage > 0) {       const status = String(get(sh, r, col.triage) || "").trim();       if (status === "Dropped") {         if (col.notes > 0) sh.getRange(r, col.notes).setNote("Marked Dropped by Ops");         if (col.severity > 0) sh.getRange(r, col.severity).setValue("Low");       }     }      // ping on High     if (col.severity > 0) {       const sev = String(get(sh, r, col.severity) || "");       if (sev.toLowerCase() === "high") {         const who   = col.who   > 0 ? String(get(sh, r, col.who)   || "") : "";         const links = col.links > 0 ? String(get(sh, r, col.links) || "") : "";         const desc  = col.desc  > 0 ? String(get(sh, r, col.desc)  || "") : "";          pingDiscord(`ğŸš¨ **High Severity Evidence** **Name/Org:** ${who} **Links:** ${links} **Notes:** ${desc ? (desc.length>500 ? desc.slice(0,500)+'â€¦' : desc) : '(none)'} (Row ${r})`);          sendMail(OPS_EMAIL, "[VAULT] High Severity Evidence", pre(` High Severity Evidence (Row ${r})  Name/Org: ${who} Links:    ${links} Notes:    ${desc} `));       }     }   } catch (err) {     Logger.log("onEditEvidence error: " + err);   } }  // utilities function findCol(headerRow, label, startsWith) {   label = String(label);   for (var i=0;i<headerRow.length;i++){     const h = String(headerRow[i] || "");     if (startsWith ? h.startsWith(label) : h === label) return i+1;   }   return -1; } function get(sh,r,c){ return (c>0)? sh.getRange(r,c).getValue() : ""; }  function suggest(text){   const t = String(text||"").toLowerCase();   if (/(fraud|money laundering|kickback|ghost|scam|theft|embezzl|bribe|pork)/.test(t)) return "High";   if (/(nepotism|conflict|misuse|misreport|coi|irregular)/.test(t)) return "Medium";   return "Low"; }  function pingDiscord(content){   try{     if(!DISCORD_WEBHOOK) return;     UrlFetchApp.fetch(DISCORD_WEBHOOK, {       method:"post", contentType:"application/json",       payload: JSON.stringify({ username:"Vault Evidence Bot", content })     });   }catch(e){ Logger.log("Discord error: "+e); } } function sendMail(to, subject, htmlBody){   try{ if(to) MailApp.sendEmail({to, subject, htmlBody}); }catch(e){ Logger.log("Mail error: "+e); } } function pre(t){ const esc=String(t).replace(/[&<>]/g,m=>({'&':'&amp;','<':'&lt;','>':'&gt;'}[m])); return "<pre>"+esc+"</pre>"; }  // optional: menu function onOpen(){   SpreadsheetApp.getUi().createMenu("Vault Ops")     .addItem("Backfill Triage/Severity", "triageBackfillAll")     .addToUi(); } function triageBackfillAll(){   const sh = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSheet();   const header = sh.getRange(1,1,1,sh.getLastColumn()).getValues()[0];   const col = {     triage:   findCol(header, COLS.triage),     reviewed: findCol(header, COLS.reviewed),     severity: findCol(header, COLS.severity),     links:    findCol(header, COLS.links, true),     desc:     findCol(header, COLS.desc,  true)   };   const last = sh.getLastRow();   for (var r=2;r<=last;r++){     try{       const status = String(get(sh,r,col.triage)||"");       const reviewed = get(sh,r,col.reviewed);       if (status && status.toLowerCase()!=="new" && !reviewed && col.reviewed>0){         sh.getRange(r,col.reviewed).setValue(new Date());       }       if (col.severity>0){         const links=String(get(sh,r,col.links)||"");         const desc =String(get(sh,r,col.desc)||"");         sh.getRange(r,col.severity).setValue(suggest(`${links} ${desc}`));       }     }catch(_){}   } }``

**Then:**

- Save (ğŸ’¾)

- Donâ€™t runÂ `onEditEvidence`Â manually (it needs the edit event)

## **Step 1 â€“ Create the Sheet with Correct Headers**

1. Open Google Sheets â†’Â **Blank spreadsheet**Â â†’ name itÂ `Vault Vetting (Ops)`.
    
2. InÂ **row 1**, paste these headersÂ **exactly**Â (one per column):
    

`Timestamp,Email,Region (PH/PR/USA/Other),Category (NGO/Influencer/Gov/Corp/Other),Name of Individual/Organization,Links to Evidence,Brief Description,Telegram/Signal handle,Triage Status,Reviewed Date,Severity,Assigned To,Notes`

## **Step 2 â€“ Add the Apps Script**

1. Go toÂ **Extensions â†’ Apps Script**.
    
2. Delete anything in there.
    
3. Paste this code:
    

``/***** VAULT â€“ Evidence Drop Automation *****/  // CONFIG â€“ change to your own values const DISCORD_WEBHOOK = "https://discord.com/api/webhooks/XXXX/YYYY"; // your #ops-alerts webhook const OPS_EMAIL = "pimpfiles@proton.me"; // your inbox  function onEdit(e) {   if (!e || !e.range) return; // safety for manual runs    const sh = e.range.getSheet();   const header = sh.getRange(1, 1, 1, sh.getLastColumn()).getValues()[0];    const col = {     triage: header.indexOf("Triage Status") + 1,     reviewed: header.indexOf("Reviewed Date") + 1,     severity: header.indexOf("Severity") + 1,     links: header.indexOf("Links to Evidence") + 1,     desc: header.indexOf("Brief Description") + 1   };    const row = e.range.getRow();   if (row === 1) return; // skip header    // Auto-stamp Reviewed Date   if (e.range.getColumn() === col.triage && e.value) {     sh.getRange(row, col.reviewed).setValue(new Date());   }    // Auto-set Severity if blank   const sevCell = sh.getRange(row, col.severity);   if (!sevCell.getValue()) {     const text = (sh.getRange(row, col.links).getValue() + " " +                   sh.getRange(row, col.desc).getValue()).toLowerCase();     let severity = "Low";     if (text.includes("fraud") || text.includes("scam") || text.includes("money")) {       severity = "High";     } else if (text.includes("warning") || text.includes("concern")) {       severity = "Medium";     }     sevCell.setValue(severity);      if (severity === "High") {       sendDiscordAlert(sh.getRange(row, col.links).getValue(), text);       sendEmailAlert(sh.getRange(row, col.links).getValue(), text);     }   } }  function sendDiscordAlert(link, desc) {   const payload = {     content: `ğŸš¨ **High Severity Evidence**\n${link}\n${desc}`   };   UrlFetchApp.fetch(DISCORD_WEBHOOK, {     method: "post",     contentType: "application/json",     payload: JSON.stringify(payload)   }); }  function sendEmailAlert(link, desc) {   MailApp.sendEmail({     to: OPS_EMAIL,     subject: "High Severity Evidence Alert",     body: `Evidence Link: ${link}\n\nDescription:\n${desc}`   }); }``

4. ClickÂ **Save**Â (ğŸ’¾).

3. Choose:
    
    - Function:Â `onEdit`
        
    - Event source:Â **From spreadsheet**
        
    - Event type:Â **On edit**
        
4. Save & authorize.

## Do this now (2 minutes)

### 1) Paste this whole code intoÂ **Extensions â†’ Apps Script**Â (replace everything)

``/***** VAULT â€” Vetting Sheet (auto-add missing Ops columns + automation) *****/  // EDIT THESE const DISCORD_WEBHOOK = "https://discord.com/api/webhooks/XXXX/YYYY";  // your #ops-alerts URL const OPS_EMAIL       = "pimpfiles@proton.me";                          // your inbox  // Required Ops columns (we'll add them if missing) const REQUIRED = ["Triage Status","Reviewed Date","Severity","Assigned To","Notes"];  /** Run this ONCE: it creates any missing Ops columns on the far right */ function vaultEnsureOpsColumns(){   const sh = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSheet();   const header = sh.getRange(1,1,1,sh.getLastColumn()).getValues()[0];   const missing = REQUIRED.filter(n=>!header.includes(n));   if (missing.length === 0) return;    // insert missing columns at the far right   sh.insertColumnsAfter(sh.getLastColumn(), missing.length);   const startCol = sh.getLastColumn() - missing.length + 1;   sh.getRange(1, startCol, 1, missing.length).setValues([missing]);    // Optional: simple dropdowns for new columns (works because these are NOT form-typed)   try {     const triCol = header.concat(missing).indexOf("Triage Status") + 1;     const sevCol = header.concat(missing).indexOf("Severity") + 1;     if (triCol > 0) sh.getRange(2, triCol, sh.getMaxRows()-1, 1)       .setDataValidation(SpreadsheetApp.newDataValidation()         .requireValueInList(["New","In Review","Approved","Dropped"], true).build());     if (sevCol > 0) sh.getRange(2, sevCol, sh.getMaxRows()-1, 1)       .setDataValidation(SpreadsheetApp.newDataValidation()         .requireValueInList(["Low","Medium","High"], true).build());   } catch(_) {} }  /** Main automation â€” add trigger: From spreadsheet â†’ On edit */ function onEditEvidence(e){   const sh = (e && e.range) ? e.range.getSheet() : SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSheet();   if (!sh) return;    const header = sh.getRange(1,1,1,sh.getLastColumn()).getValues()[0];   const col = mapCols(header, {     triage: "Triage Status",     reviewed: "Reviewed Date",     severity: "Severity",     links: "Links to Evidence",     desc: "Brief Description",     who: "Name of Individual/Organization",     notes: "Notes"   });    const r = (e && e.range) ? e.range.getRow() : 2;   const c = (e && e.range) ? e.range.getColumn() : 1;   if (r === 1) return;    // stamp date when triage changes   if (c === col.triage && col.reviewed){     sh.getRange(r, col.reviewed).setValue(new Date());   }    // suggest severity when links/desc/triage touched   if (col.severity && [col.links, col.desc, col.triage].includes(c)){     const links = get(sh,r,col.links), desc = get(sh,r,col.desc);     sh.getRange(r, col.severity).setValue(suggest(`${links} ${desc}`));   }    // normalize links to https://   if (c === col.links && col.links){     const v = String(get(sh,r,col.links)||"").trim();     if (v && !/^https?:\/\//i.test(v)) sh.getRange(r, col.links).setValue("https://" + v);   }    // alert on High   if (col.severity){     const sev = String(get(sh,r,col.severity)||"").toLowerCase();     if (sev === "high"){       const who = col.who ? String(get(sh,r,col.who)||"") : "";       const links = col.links ? String(get(sh,r,col.links)||"") : "";       const desc = col.desc ? String(get(sh,r,col.desc)||"") : "";       pingDiscord(`ğŸš¨ **High Severity Vetting** **Name/Org:** ${who} **Links:** ${links} **Notes:** ${desc ? (desc.length>500 ? desc.slice(0,500)+'â€¦' : desc) : '(none)'} (Row ${r})`);       sendMail(OPS_EMAIL, "[VAULT] High Severity Vetting",         pre(`Name/Org: ${who}\nLinks: ${links}\nNotes: ${desc}`));     }   } }  /** Helpers */ function mapCols(header, wanted){   const ix = (name)=> header.indexOf(name) + 1;   const out = {};   Object.keys(wanted).forEach(k=>{     out[k] = ix(wanted[k]) || 0;   });   return out; } function get(sh,r,c){ return (c>0) ? sh.getRange(r,c).getValue() : ""; } function suggest(t){   t = String(t||"").toLowerCase();   if (/(fraud|money laundering|kickback|ghost|scam|theft|embezzl|bribe|pork)/.test(t)) return "High";   if (/(nepotism|conflict|misuse|misreport|coi|irregular)/.test(t)) return "Medium";   return "Low"; } function pingDiscord(content){   try{     if(!DISCORD_WEBHOOK) return;     UrlFetchApp.fetch(DISCORD_WEBHOOK, {       method:"post", contentType:"application/json",       payload: JSON.stringify({ username:"Vault Vetting Bot", content })     });   }catch(e){ Logger.log("Discord error: "+e); } } function sendMail(to, subject, htmlBody){ try{ if(to) MailApp.sendEmail({to, subject, htmlBody}); }catch(e){} } function pre(t){ const esc=String(t).replace(/[&<>]/g,m=>({'&':'&amp;','<':'&lt;','>':'&gt;'}[m])); return "<pre>"+esc+"</pre>"; }  /** Quick test helper (optional) */ function simulate(){ vaultEnsureOpsColumns(); onEditEvidence({range: SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSheet().getRange(2,1)}); }``

### 2) ClickÂ **Save**.

### 3) RunÂ **vaultEnsureOpsColumns()**Â once

- In the editorâ€™s top dropdown, chooseÂ `vaultEnsureOpsColumns`Â â†’Â **Run**Â â†’ authorize.
    
- This creates the missing Ops columns on the far right:
    
    - `Triage Status`,Â `Reviewed Date`,Â `Severity`,Â `Assigned To`,Â `Notes`

### B) Paste this Apps Script (handles stamps + severity + pings)

Sheet â†’Â **Extensions â†’ Apps Script**Â â†’ replace everything with:

``/***** VAULT â€” Vetting (Form Responses 1 + Ops columns at right) *****/  // EDIT THESE const DISCORD_WEBHOOK = "https://discord.com/api/webhooks/XXXX/YYYY";  // your #ops-alerts URL const OPS_EMAIL       = "pimpfiles@proton.me";                          // your inbox  // exact Ops headers you just added const COLS = {   triage:   "Triage Status",   reviewed: "Reviewed Date",   severity: "Severity",   notes:    "Notes",   who:      "Name of Individual/Organization",   links:    "Links to Evidence",   desc:     "Brief Description" };  function onEdit(e) {   const sh = (e && e.range) ? e.range.getSheet() : SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSheet();   if (!sh) return;   const header = sh.getRange(1,1,1,sh.getLastColumn()).getValues()[0];   const col = map(header, COLS);    const r = (e && e.range) ? e.range.getRow() : 2;   const c = (e && e.range) ? e.range.getColumn() : 1;   if (r === 1) return;    // stamp Reviewed Date when Triage changes   if (c === col.triage && col.reviewed) {     sh.getRange(r, col.reviewed).setValue(new Date());   }    // normalize links to https:// when edited   if (c === col.links && col.links) {     const v = String(get(sh,r,col.links)||"").trim();     if (v && !/^https?:\/\//i.test(v)) sh.getRange(r, col.links).setValue("https://" + v);   }    // suggest severity when links/description/triage touched   if (col.severity && [col.links, col.desc, col.triage].includes(c)) {     const text = (get(sh,r,col.links) + " " + get(sh,r,col.desc)).toLowerCase();     const sev = score(text);     sh.getRange(r, col.severity).setValue(sev);      // alert on High     if (sev === "High") {       const who   = col.who ? String(get(sh,r,col.who)||"") : "";       const links = col.links ? String(get(sh,r,col.links)||"") : "";       const desc  = col.desc ? String(get(sh,r,col.desc)||"") : "";       pingDiscord(`ğŸš¨ **High Severity Vetting** **Name/Org:** ${who} **Links:** ${links} **Notes:** ${desc ? (desc.length>500 ? desc.slice(0,500)+'â€¦' : desc) : '(none)'} (Row ${r})`);       mail(OPS_EMAIL, "[VAULT] High Severity Vetting",            pre(`Name/Org: ${who}\nLinks: ${links}\nNotes: ${desc}`));     }   } }  // helpers function map(header, names) {   const idx = n => header.indexOf(n) + 1;   const out = {};   Object.keys(names).forEach(k => out[k] = idx(names[k]) || 0);   return out; } function get(sh,r,c){ return (c>0)? sh.getRange(r,c).getValue() : ""; } function score(t){   if (/(fraud|money laundering|kickback|ghost|scam|theft|embezzl|bribe|pork)/.test(t)) return "High";   if (/(nepotism|conflict|misuse|misreport|coi|irregular)/.test(t)) return "Medium";   return "Low"; } function pingDiscord(content){   try{ if(!DISCORD_WEBHOOK) return;     UrlFetchApp.fetch(DISCORD_WEBHOOK, {method:"post",contentType:"application/json",       payload: JSON.stringify({username:"Vault Vetting Bot", content})});   }catch(e){ Logger.log("Discord error: "+e); } } function mail(to, subject, htmlBody){ try{ if(to) MailApp.sendEmail({to, subject, htmlBody}); }catch(e){} } function pre(t){ const esc=String(t).replace(/[&<>]/g,m=>({'&':'&amp;','<':'&lt;','>':'&gt;'}[m])); return "<pre>"+esc+"</pre>"; }``

**Edit two lines at top:**Â put your realÂ `DISCORD_WEBHOOK`Â andÂ `OPS_EMAIL`.

# [SCRIPT]Â `vault_open`

Morning one-shot. Pull latest, seed todayâ€™s log, open it.

`#!/bin/bash set -euo pipefail  # Load config ENV_FILE="$HOME/Documents/PovertyPimpsVault/scripts/.env.vault" [[ -f "$ENV_FILE" ]] && source "$ENV_FILE" || {   echo "âŒ Missing $ENV_FILE â€” create it from the template I provided."; exit 1; }  # Ensure folders mkdir -p "$OPS_LOGS" "$BACKUPS_DIR"  echo "â–¶ï¸ OPEN: Pulling latest site repoâ€¦" if [[ -d "$SITE_REPO/.git" ]]; then   git -C "$SITE_REPO" pull --rebase --autostash || true else   echo "â„¹ï¸ Site repo not found at $SITE_REPO (skipping git pull)." fi  # Seed todayâ€™s log (create if missing) TODAY=$(date +%Y-%m-%d) LOGFILE="$OPS_LOGS/ops_log_${TODAY}.md" if [[ ! -f "$LOGFILE" ]]; then   cat > "$LOGFILE" <<EOF # ğŸ—„ Vault Ops Log â€” ${TODAY}  ## âœ… Confirmed Actions (Ok to Go) - [ ]   ## ğŸš§ Pending / Needs Review - [ ]   ## ğŸ›  Implemented Changes -   ## ğŸ“Œ Notes / Reminders -   ## ğŸ“… Next Work Session PHT: 3:00â€“8:00 PM, break, 9:00 PMâ€“3:00 AM Main Focus:  EOF   echo "âœ… Created todayâ€™s log: $LOGFILE" else   echo "ğŸ“Œ Using existing log: $LOGFILE" fi  # Optional: open the log if [[ -n "${EDITOR_BIN:-}" ]]; then   "$EDITOR_BIN" "$LOGFILE" || true fi  echo "âœ… OPEN complete. # [SCRIPT]Â `vault_close`

Night one-shot. Stage logs, commit/push, make a dated backup, optional rclone sync.

`#!/bin/bash set -euo pipefail  # Load config ENV_FILE="$HOME/Documents/PovertyPimpsVault/scripts/.env.vault" [[ -f "$ENV_FILE" ]] && source "$ENV_FILE" || {   echo "âŒ Missing $ENV_FILE â€” create it from the template."; exit 1; }  mkdir -p "$OPS_LOGS" "$BACKUPS_DIR"  TODAY=$(date +%Y-%m-%d) TS=$(date +%Y%m%d_%H%M%S) LOGFILE="$OPS_LOGS/ops_log_${TODAY}.md"  echo "ğŸ§· CLOSE: ensuring todayâ€™s log existsâ€¦" [[ -f "$LOGFILE" ]] || echo "# ğŸ—„ Vault Ops Log â€” ${TODAY}" > "$LOGFILE"  # Commit/push logs to repo (if you want logs tracked in the site repo, copy them in first) echo "ğŸ“¦ Git add/commit/push (site repo)â€¦" if [[ -d "$SITE_REPO/.git" ]]; then   # Optionally mirror logs into the repo under /Vault_Ops_Logs   mkdir -p "$SITE_REPO/Vault_Ops_Logs"   rsync -a "$OPS_LOGS/" "$SITE_REPO/Vault_Ops_Logs/"    git -C "$SITE_REPO" add -A   git -C "$SITE_REPO" commit -m "VOLTOPS: update logs (${TODAY})" || echo "â„¹ï¸ Nothing to commit."   git -C "$SITE_REPO" push || echo "âš ï¸ Push failed (check network/creds)." else   echo "â„¹ï¸ Site repo not found at $SITE_REPO â€” skipping git stage/push." fi  # Create local backup archive of Vault Ops logs ARCHIVE="$BACKUPS_DIR/Vault_Ops_Logs_${TS}.zip" echo "ğŸ§³ Creating backup: $ARCHIVE" (cd "$OPS_LOGS" && zip -qr "$ARCHIVE" .) || echo "âš ï¸ zip failed."  # Optional: rclone sync to ProtonDrive (set RCLONE_REMOTE in .env.vault) if [[ -n "${RCLONE_REMOTE:-}" ]]; then   echo "â˜ï¸ rclone sync to $RCLONE_REMOTE â€¦"   rclone copy "$ARCHIVE" "$RCLONE_REMOTE" || echo "âš ï¸ rclone copy failed." else   echo "â„¹ï¸ RCLONE_REMOTE not set; cloud sync skipped." fi  echo "âœ… CLOSE complete. Good night, operator."`

###### ChatGPT said:

The reason you keep landing in thatÂ **`vi`Â merge message screen**Â before you even get to run your one-liner is because of howÂ `git pull`Â works.

When Git pulls changes from the remote and there are commits to merge, itÂ **pauses**Â and asks you to enter a commit message for the merge â€” and by default, it opensÂ `vi`Â (orÂ `vim`) to do that.

Thatâ€™s exactly why you see:

`Lines starting with '#' will be ignored...`

â€¦and your terminal is â€œstuckâ€ in an editor until youÂ `:wq`.

---

### How to avoid this entirely

If you want yourÂ **safe merge + push**Â toÂ _never_Â drop you intoÂ `vi`Â again, we just need to tellÂ `git pull`Â toÂ **auto-write the merge commit message**Â instead of asking you for one.

You can do thatÂ **once and for all**Â by running:

`git config --global pull.rebase false git config --global core.editor "true"`

TheÂ `core.editor "true"`Â trick tells Git toÂ _instantly accept_Â the default commit message without opening an editor.

---

### New one-liner (no vi, no interruptions)

Hereâ€™s your updatedÂ **Vault sync**Â line:

`git add -A && git commit -m "DailyOps: sync join.html + gate.html updates" && git pull --no-edit origin main --no-rebase && git push origin main`

Key change:  
`git pull --no-edit`Â â†’ skips the editor, uses the default merge commit message, and keeps you moving.

---

If you want, I can also wrap that into aÂ `VaultSync.command`Â file so itâ€™s aÂ **double-click button on your Desktop**Â â€” no typing, noÂ `vi`, no stalls.

## 1) Bust the cache

    `https://papiricanpi.github.io/gate.html?v=2`

### A. Compute your passcodeâ€™s SHA-256 (in the browser console)

### B. Compare to the pageâ€™s EXPECTED_HASH

Should I use ftp

###### ChatGPT said:

Papi, forÂ **The Vault**Â and yourÂ **TruthBot Zero / PPS ops**, plain FTP is like leaving the vault door open and putting a neon sign outside sayingÂ _â€œcome rob me.â€_

Hereâ€™s the quick lowdown:

---

## **ğŸš« Why you should NOT use plain FTP**

- **No encryption**Â â€” your files (and login credentials) travel in plain text. Anyone sniffing network traffic (ISP, bad actor, government) can seeÂ _everything_.
    
- **Easy to hijack**Â â€” credentials can be intercepted and re-used.
    
- **Zero integrity checks**Â â€” files could be altered in transit without you knowing.
    

---

## **âœ… Safer alternatives for your mission**

1. **SFTP (SSH File Transfer Protocol)**
    
    - Encrypts everything (login + data).
        
    - Uses the same keys/passwords as SSH.
        
    - Works with any secure hosting or server.
        
2. **FTPS (FTP over SSL/TLS)**
    
    - Still â€œFTPâ€ but wrapped in encryption.
        
    - Good if youâ€™re dealing with legacy systems that only â€œspeak FTP.â€
        
3. **rsync over SSH**Â (my favorite for The Vault)
    
    - Lets you sync local and remote folders securely.
        
    - Can run as a one-liner or scheduled script.
        
    - Verifies file integrity after transfer.
        
4. **Proton Drive or Encrypted Cloud Sync**
    
    - Youâ€™re already using Proton for The Vault â€” encrypted end-to-end, no FTP risks.
        

---

## **ğŸ’¡ My Recommendation for The Vault**

- ForÂ **internal ops**Â â†’ rsync over SSH or Proton Drive.
    
- ForÂ **public site updates**Â â†’ SFTP via a secure client likeÂ **Cyberduck**,Â **Transmit**, or CLI.
    
- ForÂ **collaborators**Â â†’ only give SFTP keys, never full account logins.
    
- Keep anÂ **offline backup**Â always â€” trust nothing 100%.
    

---

# 1) Config file â€”Â `~/.vaultsync.env`

Edit the values inÂ **ALL CAPS**Â to match your server.

`cat > ~/.vaultsync.env <<'EOF' # ===== Vault Secure Sync (.env) ===== # SSH connection SSH_USER="YOUR_SSH_USER" SSH_HOST="YOUR_SERVER_HOST_OR_IP" SSH_PORT="22"  # Remote base folder on server (create it once) REMOTE_BASE="/home/YOUR_SSH_USER/vault"  # Local paths (change if different) LOCAL_SITE="$HOME/Documents/PovertyPimpsVault/papiricanpi.github.io" LOCAL_MARKETING="$HOME/Documents/PovertyPimpsVault/Legacy_Files/Marketing_Strategy"  # Remote paths (auto-created on first push) REMOTE_SITE="$REMOTE_BASE/site" REMOTE_MARKETING="$REMOTE_BASE/marketing_strategy"  # Logging LOG_DIR="$HOME/Documents/PovertyPimpsVault/Vault_Ops_Logs"  # Rsync exclude patterns (space-separated or file path) RSYNC_EXCLUDES="*.DS_Store .git node_modules .obsidian .Trash" EOF`

> KeepÂ `~/.vaultsync.env`Â private. It holds endpoints, not passwords.

---

# 2) The script â€”Â `~/Documents/PovertyPimpsVault/scripts/vault_sync_secure`

`cat > ~/Documents/PovertyPimpsVault/scripts/vault_sync_secure <<'EOF' #!/bin/zsh set -euo pipefail  # Load config if [[ -f "$HOME/.vaultsync.env" ]]; then   source "$HOME/.vaultsync.env" else   echo "âŒ Missing ~/.vaultsync.env"; exit 1 fi  # Timestamp + log TS=$(date +"%Y-%m-%d_%H-%M-%S") mkdir -p "$LOG_DIR" LOG="$LOG_DIR/sync_$TS.log"  # SSH/rsync helpers SSH_OPTS=(-p "$SSH_PORT" -o StrictHostKeyChecking=yes -o UserKnownHostsFile="$HOME/.ssh/known_hosts") RSYNC_SSH=(-e "ssh ${SSH_OPTS[*]}") RSYNC_BASE=(-azP --delete --chmod=Du=rwx,Dg=rx,Do= --mkpath "${RSYNC_SSH[@]}")  # Build exclude args EXCLUDES=() for pat in $RSYNC_EXCLUDES; do   EXCLUDES+=(--exclude="$pat") done  function log() { printf "%s %s\n" "$(date +"%H:%M:%S")" "$*" | tee -a "$LOG"; }  function ensure_remote_dirs() {   ssh "${SSH_OPTS[@]}" "${SSH_USER}@${SSH_HOST}" "mkdir -p '$REMOTE_SITE' '$REMOTE_MARKETING' '$REMOTE_BASE/.archives'" }  function push_site() {   log "â¬†ï¸  Push: SITE  ($LOCAL_SITE -> $REMOTE_SITE)"   rsync "${RSYNC_BASE[@]}" "${EXCLUDES[@]}" "$LOCAL_SITE/" "${SSH_USER}@${SSH_HOST}:$REMOTE_SITE/" | tee -a "$LOG" }  function push_marketing() {   log "â¬†ï¸  Push: MARKETING  ($LOCAL_MARKETING -> $REMOTE_MARKETING)"   rsync "${RSYNC_BASE[@]}" "${EXCLUDES[@]}" "$LOCAL_MARKETING/" "${SSH_USER}@${SSH_HOST}:$REMOTE_MARKETING/" | tee -a "$LOG" }  function pull_site() {   log "â¬‡ï¸  Pull: SITE  ($REMOTE_SITE -> $LOCAL_SITE)"   rsync "${RSYNC_BASE[@]}" "${EXCLUDES[@]}" "${SSH_USER}@${SSH_HOST}:$REMOTE_SITE/" "$LOCAL_SITE/" | tee -a "$LOG" }  function pull_marketing() {   log "â¬‡ï¸  Pull: MARKETING  ($REMOTE_MARKETING -> $LOCAL_MARKETING)"   rsync "${RSYNC_BASE[@]}" "${EXCLUDES[@]}" "${SSH_USER}@${SSH_HOST}:$REMOTE_MARKETING/" "$LOCAL_MARKETING/" | tee -a "$LOG" }  function usage() {   cat <<USAGE Usage: $(basename "$0") [push|pull] [site|marketing|both]   Default: push both  Examples:   $(basename "$0") push site   $(basename "$0") push marketing   $(basename "$0") pull both USAGE }  # Known-hosts pin (first-time: this will add fingerprint) ssh-keyscan -p "$SSH_PORT" "$SSH_HOST" >> "$HOME/.ssh/known_hosts" 2>/dev/null || true  # Parse args ACTION="${1:-push}" TARGET="${2:-both}"  ensure_remote_dirs  case "$ACTION:$TARGET" in   push:site)       push_site ;;   push:marketing)  push_marketing ;;   push:both|push:*) push_site; push_marketing ;;   pull:site)       pull_site ;;   pull:marketing)  pull_marketing ;;   pull:both|pull:*) pull_site; pull_marketing ;;   *) usage; exit 1 ;; esac  log "âœ… Done. Log saved: $LOG" echo "âœ… Done. Log saved: $LOG" EOF  chmod +x ~/Documents/PovertyPimpsVault/scripts/vault_sync_secure`

# 3) Apps Script: Discord + Telegram auto-notify on submit

This script catches Google Form submissions andÂ **sends to Discord (#ops-alerts), Telegram (invite/broadcast), and email ops**. It also sanity-checks the most important fields and labels any that are empty.

### How to install

1. Open theÂ **responses Sheet**Â (the spreadsheet tied to your Form).
    
2. Extensions â†’Â **Apps Script**.
    
3. Delete any code, paste the code below asÂ `Code.gs`.
    
4. Edit theÂ **CONFIG**Â block (webhook, email, telegram).
    
5. Triggers â†’Â **+ Add Trigger**Â â†’ chooseÂ `onFormSubmit`Â â†’  
    _From spreadsheet_Â â†’Â **On form submit**Â â†’ Save.
    

```/***** VAULT â€” Vetting Pipeline: Discord + Telegram + Email *****/  // === CONFIG === const DISCORD_WEBHOOK = "https://discord.com/api/webhooks/XXXXXXXX/XXXXXXXXXXXXXXXX"; // #ops-alerts const OPS_EMAIL       = "pimpfiles@proton.me";  // Telegram: create @BotFather bot, get token; add bot to your private channel/group as Admin. // Use @RawDataBot or this script once to learn chat ID. const TG_BOT_TOKEN = "123456789:AA...";           // your bot token const TG_CHAT_ID   = "-1001234567890";            // channel/group id (negative for supergroup/channel)  // Optional: send an auto-reply to the applicant (if "Email" header exists) const REPLY_TO_APPLICANT = false;  // === MAIN === function onFormSubmit(e) {   try {     // Map headers â†’ values     const sh = e.range.getSheet();     const header = sh.getRange(1,1,1, sh.getLastColumn()).getValues()[0];     const row = e.range.getRow();     const values = sh.getRange(row,1,1, header.length).getValues()[0];      const data = {};     header.forEach((h, i) => data[h] = values[i]);      // Quick sanity flags (adjust field names to yours)     const must = ["Full Name","Alias / Handle","Role","Email","Share 1â€“3 links that show your signal (thread, post, or receipts)","I agree to follow the Vault Oath","No doxxing, no incitement, no illegal ops"];     const missing = must.filter(k => !data[k] || String(data[k]).trim() === "");      // Build Discord message     const lines = [       `**New Vetting Request**`,       `**Name:** ${s(data["Full Name"]) || "N/A"}`,       `**Alias:** ${s(data["Alias / Handle"]) || "N/A"}`,       `**Role:** ${s(data["Role"]) || "N/A"}`,       `**Email:** ${s(data["Email"]) || "N/A"}`,       `**Links:** ${s(data["Share 1â€“3 links that show your signal (thread, post, or receipts)"]) || "N/A"}`,       `**Rules OK?:** ${s(data["Can you follow our sourcing rules? (Multiple choice)"]) || "N/A"}`,       `**Oath:** ${s(data["I agree to follow the Vault Oath"]) || "N/A"}`,       `**No Doxx/Incitement:** ${s(data["No doxxing, no incitement, no illegal ops"]) || "N/A"}`,       missing.length ? `:warning: **Missing:** ${missing.join(", ")}` : `:white_check_mark: All required fields present`     ];      postDiscord(lines.join("\n"));     postTelegram(`New vetting request:\n` +       `Name: ${s(data["Full Name"]) || "N/A"}\n` +       `Alias: ${s(data["Alias / Handle"]) || "N/A"}\n` +       `Role: ${s(data["Role"]) || "N/A"}\n` +       `Email: ${s(data["Email"]) || "N/A"}\n` +       `Links: ${truncate(s(data["Share 1â€“3 links that show your signal (thread, post, or receipts)"]), 900) || "N/A"}` +       (missing.length ? `\nâš ï¸ Missing: ${missing.join(", ")}` : ``)     );      // Email ops     MailApp.sendEmail({       to: OPS_EMAIL,       subject: "New Vetting Request",       htmlBody: lines.map(escapeHtml).join("<br>")     });      // Optional: reply to applicant with a short receipt     if (REPLY_TO_APPLICANT && data["Email"]) {       MailApp.sendEmail({         to: String(data["Email"]).trim(),         subject: "The Vault â€” we got your request",         htmlBody: "Thanks â€” our mods will review and reply. Use a throwaway handle and keep receipts handy. â€” TruthBot Zero"       });     }   } catch (err) {     postDiscord(":warning: onFormSubmit error: " + err.message);     throw err;   } }  // === helpers === function s(v){ return (v===undefined || v===null) ? "" : String(v); } function truncate(str, n){ str=str||""; return str.length>n ? str.slice(0,n-1)+"â€¦" : str; } function escapeHtml(str){ return s(str).replace(/[&<>"']/g, m=>({ "&":"&amp;","<":"&lt;",">":"&gt;","\"":"&quot;","'":"&#39;" }[m])); }  function postDiscord(message){   const payload = { content: message };   UrlFetchApp.fetch(DISCORD_WEBHOOK, {     method: "post",     contentType: "application/json",     payload: JSON.stringify(payload),     muteHttpExceptions: true   }); }  function postTelegram(text){   if(!TG_BOT_TOKEN || !TG_CHAT_ID) return;   const url = `https://api.telegram.org/bot${TG_BOT_TOKEN}/sendMessage`;   const payload = { chat_id: TG_CHAT_ID, text: text, parse_mode: "HTML", disable_web_page_preview: true };   UrlFetchApp.fetch(url, {     method: "post",     contentType: "application/json",     payload: JSON.stringify(payload),     muteHttpExceptions: true   }); }  /* One-time helper to discover TG chat ID:    1) Add bot to your private channel/group as admin.    2) Post something in that channel/group.    3) Temporarily set TG_CHAT_ID="", then run getTelegramUpdates() to log IDs. */ function getTelegramUpdates(){   const url = `https://api.telegram.org/bot${TG_BOT_TOKEN}/getUpdates`;   const res = UrlFetchApp.fetch(url, { method:"get", muteHttpExceptions:true });   Logger.log(res.getContentText()); }```

**What this gives you**

- Every form submit â†’ Discord ping inÂ **#ops-alerts**.
    
- Same payload â†’ Telegram channel/group (Anonymous-style).
    
- Email receipt toÂ **pimpfiles@proton.me**.
    
- Warns if required fields look empty.
    

> **Security**: keep the Discord webhook & Telegram token in Apps Script only (not in the public repo). Never paste webhooks into GitHub.

# 5) Apps Script: Discord + Telegram + Ops email

In theÂ **Responses spreadsheet**:  
Extensions â†’Â **Apps Script**Â â†’ paste this code â†’ edit CONFIG â†’ save.  
Triggers â†’Â **+ Add Trigger**Â â†’Â `onFormSubmit`Â â†’Â _From spreadsheet_Â â†’Â **On form submit**Â â†’ Save.

```/***** VAULT â€” Vetting Pipeline: Discord + Telegram + Email *****/  // === CONFIG === const DISCORD_WEBHOOK = "PASTE_YOUR_OPS_ALERTS_WEBHOOK"; // #ops-alerts const OPS_EMAIL       = "pimpfiles@proton.me";  // Telegram bot (create via @BotFather). Add bot as Admin to your private channel/group. const TG_BOT_TOKEN = "123456789:AA...";   // your token const TG_CHAT_ID   = "-1001234567890";    // channel/group id  const REPLY_TO_APPLICANT = false; // set true to auto-email the applicant  function onFormSubmit(e){   try{     const sh = e.range.getSheet();     const header = sh.getRange(1,1,1, sh.getLastColumn()).getValues()[0];     const row = e.range.getRow();     const values = sh.getRange(row,1,1, header.length).getValues()[0];     const data = {};     header.forEach((h,i)=> data[h]=values[i]);      const must = [       "Full Name","Alias / Handle","Role","Email",       "Share 1â€“3 links that show your signal (thread, post, or receipts)",       "I agree to follow the Vault Oath","No doxxing, no incitement, no illegal ops"     ];     const missing = must.filter(k => !data[k] || String(data[k]).trim()==="");      const lines = [       `**New Vetting Request**`,       `**Name:** ${s(data["Full Name"])||"N/A"}`,       `**Alias:** ${s(data["Alias / Handle"])||"N/A"}`,       `**Role:** ${s(data["Role"])||"N/A"}`,       `**Email:** ${s(data["Email"])||"N/A"}`,       `**Links:** ${s(data["Share 1â€“3 links that show your signal (thread, post, or receipts)"])||"N/A"}`,       `**Rules OK?:** ${s(data["Can you follow our sourcing rules? (Multiple choice)"])||"N/A"}`,       `**Oath:** ${s(data["I agree to follow the Vault Oath"])||"N/A"}`,       `**No Doxx/Incitement:** ${s(data["No doxxing, no incitement, no illegal ops"])||"N/A"}`,       missing.length? `:warning: **Missing:** ${missing.join(", ")}` : `:white_check_mark: All required fields present`     ];      // Discord     postDiscord(lines.join("\n"));      // Telegram (Anonymous-style broadcast)     postTelegram(       `New vetting request:\n`+       `Name: ${s(data["Full Name"])||"N/A"}\n`+       `Alias: ${s(data["Alias / Handle"])||"N/A"}\n`+       `Role: ${s(data["Role"])||"N/A"}\n`+       `Email: ${s(data["Email"])||"N/A"}\n`+       `Links: ${truncate(s(data["Share 1â€“3 links that show your signal (thread, post, or receipts)"]),900) || "N/A"}`+       (missing.length? `\nâš ï¸ Missing: ${missing.join(", ")}` : ``)     );      // Email ops     MailApp.sendEmail({ to: OPS_EMAIL, subject: "New Vetting Request", htmlBody: lines.map(escapeHtml).join("<br>") });      // Optional: reply to applicant     if(REPLY_TO_APPLICANT && data["Email"]){       MailApp.sendEmail({         to: String(data["Email"]).trim(),         subject: "The Vault â€” we got your request",         htmlBody: "Thanks â€” our mods will review and reply. Use a throwaway handle and keep receipts handy. â€” TruthBot Zero"       });     }   }catch(err){     postDiscord(":warning: onFormSubmit error: " + err.message);     throw err;   } }  function s(v){ return (v===undefined||v===null) ? "" : String(v); } function truncate(str,n){ str=str||""; return str.length>n? str.slice(0,n-1)+"â€¦" : str; } function escapeHtml(str){ return s(str).replace(/[&<>"']/g, m=>({"&":"&amp;","<":"&lt;",">":"&gt;","\"":"&quot;","'":"&#39;"}[m])); }  function postDiscord(message){   if(!DISCORD_WEBHOOK) return;   UrlFetchApp.fetch(DISCORD_WEBHOOK,{     method:"post", contentType:"application/json",     payload: JSON.stringify({content: message}), muteHttpExceptions:true   }); }  function postTelegram(text){   if(!TG_BOT_TOKEN || !TG_CHAT_ID) return;   const url = `https://api.telegram.org/bot${TG_BOT_TOKEN}/sendMessage`;   UrlFetchApp.fetch(url,{     method:"post", contentType:"application/json",     payload: JSON.stringify({chat_id:TG_CHAT_ID, text, parse_mode:"HTML", disable_web_page_preview:true}),     muteHttpExceptions:true   }); }  /* Helper to discover Telegram chat ID (run once, check Logs):    1) Add bot to your private channel/group as Admin.    2) Post something in that channel/group.    3) Put token above, then run getTelegramUpdates() and check Apps Script logs. */ function getTelegramUpdates(){   const url = `https://api.telegram.org/bot${TG_BOT_TOKEN}/getUpdates`;   const res = UrlFetchApp.fetch(url, {method:"get", muteHttpExceptions:true});   Logger.log(res.getContentText()); }```

> **Security**: keep webhook, bot token, and chat IDÂ **only**Â in Apps Script. Donâ€™t push to GitHub.

# ğŸ§© Paste this entire script asÂ `Code.gs`

``/***********************  * VAULT OPS AUTOMATION  * - Form submit -> Discord ping + Telegram broadcast summary  * - Manual vetting: set Status = APPROVED -> DM Telegram invite  * - RSS -> auto-post to Discord + Telegram  ***********************/  /* ========= CONFIG ========= */ const CFG = {   // Discord   DISCORD_OPS_WEBHOOK: "https://discord.com/api/webhooks/XXXXXXXX/XXXXXXXXXXXXXXXX", // #ops-alerts (vetting)   DISCORD_BROADCAST_WEBHOOK: "https://discord.com/api/webhooks/YYYYYYYY/YYYYYYYYYYYY", // public/broadcast channel (optional)    // Telegram   TG_BOT_TOKEN: "123456789:AA...",      // @BotFather token   TG_INVITE_DM_TEXT: "Youâ€™ve been approved for The Vault. Use this private invite:\n\n{INVITE}\n\nStay anon. No doxx. â€” TruthBot Zero",    TG_GROUP_INVITE_LINK: "https://t.me/+YOUR_INVITE_HASH",   // the link you give to approved users   TG_BROADCAST_CHAT_ID: "-1001234567890", // your broadcast channel/group ID (negative for channels/supergroups)    // Sheet headers (must match Form questions)   HEADERS: {     FULLNAME: "Full Name",     ALIAS: "Alias / Handle",     ROLE: "Role",     EMAIL: "Email",     TELEGRAM: "Telegram/Signal handle",     LINKS: "Share 1â€“3 links that show your signal (thread, post, or receipts)",     RULES_OK: "Can you follow our sourcing rules? (Multiple choice)",     OATH: "I agree to follow the Vault Oath",     NO_DOXX: "No doxxing, no incitement, no illegal ops",     STATUS: "Status",     NOTES: "Ops Notes"   },    // RSS feeds (add more as needed)   RSS_FEEDS: [     "https://YOUR-SUBSTACK.substack.com/feed",     "https://MASTODON.INSTANCE/@yourhandle.rss"   ],    // Broadcast prefix   RSS_PREFIX: "ğŸ“¢ New post:", };  /* ========= FORM SUBMIT: Discord + Telegram summary ========= */ function onFormSubmit(e) {   try {     const sh = e.range.getSheet();     const header = sh.getRange(1,1,1, sh.getLastColumn()).getValues()[0];     const row = e.range.getRow();     const values = sh.getRange(row,1,1, header.length).getValues()[0];      const H = CFG.HEADERS;     const data = mapRow(header, values);      const must = [H.ALIAS, H.ROLE, H.EMAIL, H.TELEGRAM, H.LINKS, H.OATH, H.NO_DOXX];     const missing = must.filter(k => !hasValue(data[k]));      // Ping Discord ops     const disc = [       `**New Vetting Request**`,       `**Alias:** ${safe(data[H.ALIAS]) || "N/A"}`,       data[H.FULLNAME] ? `**Name:** ${safe(data[H.FULLNAME])}` : null,       `**Role:** ${safe(data[H.ROLE]) || "N/A"}`,       `**Email:** ${safe(data[H.EMAIL]) || "N/A"}`,       `**Telegram:** ${fmtTelegram(data[H.TELEGRAM]) || "N/A"}`,       `**Links:** ${truncate(safe(data[H.LINKS]), 900) || "N/A"}`,       `**Rules OK?:** ${safe(data[H.RULES_OK]) || "N/A"}`,       `**Oath:** ${safe(data[H.OATH]) || "N/A"}`,       `**No Doxx/Incitement:** ${safe(data[H.NO_DOXX]) || "N/A"}`,       missing.length ? `:warning: **Missing:** ${missing.join(", ")}` : `:white_check_mark: All required fields present`,       `_Set **${H.STATUS}** to **APPROVED** in the sheet to auto-DM the Telegram invite._`     ].filter(Boolean).join("\n");      postDiscord(CFG.DISCORD_OPS_WEBHOOK, disc);      // Telegram broadcast summary (optional; comment out if you don't want)     if (CFG.TG_BOT_TOKEN && CFG.TG_BROADCAST_CHAT_ID) {       const msg =          "ğŸ“ New vetting request\n" +         `Alias: ${safe(data[H.ALIAS]) || "N/A"}\n` +         `Role: ${safe(data[H.ROLE]) || "N/A"}\n` +         `Telegram: ${fmtTelegram(data[H.TELEGRAM]) || "N/A"}\n` +         `Links: ${truncate(safe(data[H.LINKS]), 600) || "N/A"}`;       tgSend(CFG.TG_BOT_TOKEN, CFG.TG_BROADCAST_CHAT_ID, msg);     }      // Ensure STATUS/NOTES columns exist (for first run convenience)     ensureOpsColumns(sh, header, [H.STATUS, H.NOTES]);    } catch (err) {     postDiscord(CFG.DISCORD_OPS_WEBHOOK, ":warning: onFormSubmit error: " + err.message);     throw err;   } }  /* ========= STATUS CHANGE: approve -> DM Telegram invite ========= */ function onStatusChange(e) {   try {     const sh = e.source.getActiveSheet();     const H = CFG.HEADERS;      // Only react on the Responses sheet     const firstRow = sh.getRange(1,1,1, sh.getLastColumn()).getValues()[0];     if (!firstRow.includes(H.STATUS)) return;      const row = e.range.getRow();     if (row === 1) return; // header row      const header = firstRow;     const values = sh.getRange(row,1,1, sh.getLastColumn()).getValues()[0];     const data = mapRow(header, values);      const status = String(data[H.STATUS] || "").trim().toUpperCase();     if (status !== "APPROVED") return;      const tgUserRaw = String(data[H.TELEGRAM] || "").trim();     const tgUser = normalizeTelegram(tgUserRaw);      if (!tgUser) {       postDiscord(CFG.DISCORD_OPS_WEBHOOK, `:warning: Approved but missing Telegram handle on row ${row}.`);       return;     }      // DM the invite (two strategies)     // A) If you know the user's numeric chat_id, use sendMessage directly to that ID (best).     // B) If not, attempt a mention with @username in your broadcast group/channel (they must be present or see public channel).     //    Safer route: include instructions to DM your bot to start (so you capture chat_id), then reply with invite.      // Here we do B + instructions:     const dmText = CFG.TG_INVITE_DM_TEXT.replace("{INVITE}", CFG.TG_GROUP_INVITE_LINK);     const broadcast = `âœ… @${tgUser} approved. ${dmText}`;      tgSend(CFG.TG_BOT_TOKEN, CFG.TG_BROADCAST_CHAT_ID, broadcast);     postDiscord(CFG.DISCORD_OPS_WEBHOOK, `:white_check_mark: Approved & invited @${tgUser}.`);    } catch (err) {     postDiscord(CFG.DISCORD_OPS_WEBHOOK, ":warning: onStatusChange error: " + err.message);     throw err;   } }  /* ========= RSS -> Discord + Telegram broadcast ========= */ function rssBroadcast() {   const done = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();   CFG.RSS_FEEDS.forEach(feedUrl => {     try {       const xml = UrlFetchApp.fetch(feedUrl, { muteHttpExceptions: true, followRedirects: true, validateHttpsCertificates: true }).getContentText();       const doc = XmlService.parse(xml);       const root = doc.getRootElement();        const channel = root.getChild("channel");       if (!channel) return;       const items = channel.getChildren("item") || [];        items.slice(0,5).forEach(item => {         const title = textOf(item, "title");         const link = textOf(item, "link");         const guid = textOf(item, "guid") || link;          const key = "rss:" + guid;         if (done.getProperty(key)) return; // already posted          const msg = `${CFG.RSS_PREFIX} ${title}\n${link}`;         if (CFG.DISCORD_BROADCAST_WEBHOOK) postDiscord(CFG.DISCORD_BROADCAST_WEBHOOK, msg);         if (CFG.TG_BOT_TOKEN && CFG.TG_BROADCAST_CHAT_ID) tgSend(CFG.TG_BOT_TOKEN, CFG.TG_BROADCAST_CHAT_ID, msg);          done.setProperty(key, "1");       });     } catch (err) {       postDiscord(CFG.DISCORD_OPS_WEBHOOK, ":warning: rssBroadcast error: " + err.message + " (" + feedUrl + ")");     }   }); }  /* ========= helpers ========= */ function mapRow(header, values){   const obj = {};   header.forEach((h,i)=> obj[h] = values[i]);   return obj; } function hasValue(v){ return !(v===undefined || v===null || String(v).trim()===""); } function safe(v){ return v===undefined || v===null ? "" : String(v); } function truncate(str,n){ str = str || ""; return str.length>n ? (str.slice(0,n-1)+"â€¦") : str; } function textOf(parent, childName){ const c = parent.getChild(childName); return c ? c.getText() : ""; } function fmtTelegram(v){ v = safe(v).trim(); if(!v) return ""; return v.startsWith("@")? v : "@"+v; } function normalizeTelegram(v){ v = safe(v).replace(/^@+/, "").replace(/\s+/g,"").trim(); return v || ""; }  function postDiscord(webhook, content){   if(!webhook) return;   const payload = { content: content };   UrlFetchApp.fetch(webhook, {     method: "post",     contentType: "application/json",     payload: JSON.stringify(payload),     muteHttpExceptions: true   }); }  function tgSend(token, chatId, text){   if(!token || !chatId) return;   const url = `https://api.telegram.org/bot${token}/sendMessage`;   UrlFetchApp.fetch(url, {     method: "post",     contentType: "application/json",     payload: JSON.stringify({ chat_id: chatId, text: text, parse_mode: "HTML", disable_web_page_preview: true }),     muteHttpExceptions: true   }); }  /* Ensure Status/Notes columns exist (appends if missing) */ function ensureOpsColumns(sh, header, need){   const missing = need.filter(n => !header.includes(n));   if (!missing.length) return;   sh.insertColumnsAfter(header.length, missing.length);   const newHeader = header.concat(missing);   sh.getRange(1,1,1,newHeader.length).setValues([newHeader]); }``

# A) Google Sheets: â€œApproveâ€ checkboxÂ **and**Â menu button

## 1) Add the â€œApprovedâ€ checkbox column (once)

In theÂ **Responses**Â sheet:

- Insert a new column at the far right.
    
- Header:Â **Approved**
    
- Data â†’Â **Data validation**Â â†’Â **Checkbox**Â (Unchecked = FALSE, Checked = TRUE)
    

Keep your existingÂ **Status**Â column too (weâ€™ll auto-fill it for audit).

## 2) Paste this Apps Script (replaces what you have)

Extensions â†’Â **Apps Script**Â â†’ replaceÂ `Code.gs`Â with this, then edit the 3 secrets inÂ **Script Properties**Â (instructions below).

``/***********************  * VAULT OPS â€” One-Click Approvals  * - Form submit -> Discord ping + (optional) TG broadcast summary  * - Tick "Approved" checkbox -> sets Status=APPROVED -> posts DM-style approval to TG broadcast with invite text  * - Custom menu: Vault Ops -> Approve selected / RSS broadcast now  * - RSS -> periodic broadcast to TG + Discord  ***********************/  /* ======= CONFIG (column headers) ======= */ const H = {   FULLNAME: "Full Name",   ALIAS: "Alias / Handle",   ROLE: "Role",   EMAIL: "Email",   TELEGRAM: "Telegram/Signal handle",   LINKS: "Share 1â€“3 links that show your signal (thread, post, or receipts)",   RULES_OK: "Can you follow our sourcing rules? (Multiple choice)",   OATH: "I agree to follow the Vault Oath",   NODOXX: "No doxxing, no incitement, no illegal ops",   STATUS: "Status",   NOTES: "Ops Notes",   APPROVED: "Approved" // checkbox column (TRUE/FALSE) };  /* ======= RSS feeds ======= */ const RSS_FEEDS = [   "https://povertypimpslayer.substack.com/feed" ];  /* ======= Secrets from Script Properties =======    Set these via: Apps Script editor â†’ Project Settings (gear) â†’ Script properties    Keys:      DISCORD_OPS_WEBHOOK      DISCORD_BROADCAST_WEBHOOK  (optional)      TG_BOT_TOKEN      TG_BROADCAST_CHAT_ID      TG_GROUP_INVITE_LINK      OPS_EMAIL */ function S_(k){ return PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().getProperty(k) || ""; }  /* ======= UI menu ======= */ function onOpen(){   SpreadsheetApp.getUi()     .createMenu("Vault Ops")     .addItem("Approve selected (DM invite)", "approveSelected")     .addSeparator()     .addItem("RSS broadcast now", "rssBroadcast")     .addToUi(); }  /* ======= FORM SUBMIT -> ops pings ======= */ function onFormSubmit(e){   try{     const sh = e.range.getSheet();     const header = sh.getRange(1,1,1,sh.getLastColumn()).getValues()[0];     const row = e.range.getRow();     const values = sh.getRange(row,1,1,header.length).getValues()[0];     const data  = mapRow(header, values);      ensureOpsColumns(sh, header, [H.STATUS, H.NOTES, H.APPROVED]);      const missing = [H.ALIAS,H.ROLE,H.EMAIL,H.TELEGRAM,H.LINKS,H.OATH,H.NODOXX]       .filter(k => !hasValue(data[k]));      const lines = [       `**New Vetting Request**`,       line("Alias", data[H.ALIAS]),       data[H.FULLNAME]? line("Name", data[H.FULLNAME]) : null,       line("Role", data[H.ROLE]),       line("Email", data[H.EMAIL]),       line("Telegram", fmtTelegram(data[H.TELEGRAM])),       line("Links", truncate(data[H.LINKS], 900)),       line("Rules OK?", data[H.RULES_OK]),       line("Oath", data[H.OATH]),       line("No Doxx/Incitement", data[H.NODOXX]),       missing.length ? `:warning: **Missing:** ${missing.join(", ")}` : `:white_check_mark: All required fields present`,       `_Tick **${H.APPROVED}** to auto-invite or use **Vault Ops â†’ Approve selected**._`     ].filter(Boolean).join("\n");      postDiscord(S_("DISCORD_OPS_WEBHOOK"), lines);      // Optional: TG broadcast summary (comment out if you donâ€™t want)     const tgMsg =       "ğŸ“ New vetting request\n" +       `Alias: ${safe(data[H.ALIAS])||"N/A"}\n` +       `Role: ${safe(data[H.ROLE])||"N/A"}\n` +       `Telegram: ${fmtTelegram(data[H.TELEGRAM])||"N/A"}\n` +       `Links: ${truncate(safe(data[H.LINKS]), 600) || "N/A"}`;     if (S_("TG_BOT_TOKEN") && S_("TG_BROADCAST_CHAT_ID")) {       tgSend(S_("TG_BOT_TOKEN"), S_("TG_BROADCAST_CHAT_ID"), tgMsg);     }    }catch(err){     postDiscord(S_("DISCORD_OPS_WEBHOOK"), ":warning: onFormSubmit error: "+err.message);     throw err;   } }  /* ======= CHECKBOX workflow: approve when Approved flips TRUE ======= */ function onEdit(e){   try{     const sh = e.range.getSheet();     const header = sh.getRange(1,1,1, sh.getLastColumn()).getValues()[0];     if (!header.includes(H.APPROVED)) return;      const row = e.range.getRow();     if (row === 1) return;      const col = e.range.getColumn();     const idxApproved = header.indexOf(H.APPROVED)+1;     if (col !== idxApproved) return;      const values = sh.getRange(row,1,1, header.length).getValues()[0];     const data   = mapRow(header, values);     const approved = String(data[H.APPROVED]).toLowerCase() === "true";      if (approved) inviteRow_(sh, header, row, data); // do the thing   }catch(err){     postDiscord(S_("DISCORD_OPS_WEBHOOK"), ":warning: onEdit error: "+err.message);   } }  /* ======= Menu: Approve selected rows ======= */ function approveSelected(){   const sh = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSheet();   const header = sh.getRange(1,1,1, sh.getLastColumn()).getValues()[0];   const sel = sh.getActiveRange();   const rows = sel ? sel.getRow() : 2;   const num  = sel ? sel.getNumRows() : 1;    for (let i=0;i<num;i++){     const r = rows + i;     if (r === 1) continue;     const values = sh.getRange(r,1,1, header.length).getValues()[0];     const data   = mapRow(header, values);     inviteRow_(sh, header, r, data);   } }  /* ======= Invite single row (called by onEdit or menu) ======= */ function inviteRow_(sh, header, row, data){   const alias = safe(data[H.ALIAS]);   const tgUser = normalizeTelegram(data[H.TELEGRAM]);   if (!tgUser){     postDiscord(S_("DISCORD_OPS_WEBHOOK"), `:warning: Missing Telegram handle on row ${row} (alias: ${alias||"N/A"}).`);     return;   }    // mark Status=APPROVED (audit)   const idxStatus = header.indexOf(H.STATUS)+1;   if (idxStatus>0) sh.getRange(row, idxStatus).setValue("APPROVED");    const dmText = `âœ… @${tgUser} approved.\n` +                  `Youâ€™ve been approved for The Vault. Use this private invite:\n\n${S_("TG_GROUP_INVITE_LINK")}\n\n` +                  `Stay anon. No doxx. â€” TruthBot Zero`;    // Broadcast mention with invite text (works if user can see the channel)   tgSend(S_("TG_BOT_TOKEN"), S_("TG_BROADCAST_CHAT_ID"), dmText);    postDiscord(S_("DISCORD_OPS_WEBHOOK"), `:white_check_mark: Approved & invited @${tgUser} (row ${row}).`); }  /* ======= RSS -> broadcast to TG + Discord ======= */ function rssBroadcast(){   const done = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();   RSS_FEEDS.forEach(feedUrl=>{     try{       const xml = UrlFetchApp.fetch(feedUrl, {muteHttpExceptions:true, followRedirects:true}).getContentText();       const doc = XmlService.parse(xml);       const channel = doc.getRootElement().getChild("channel");       if(!channel) return;       const items = channel.getChildren("item") || [];       items.slice(0,5).forEach(item=>{         const title = textOf(item,"title");         const link  = textOf(item,"link");         const guid  = textOf(item,"guid") || link;         const key   = "rss:"+guid;         if (done.getProperty(key)) return;          const msg = `ğŸ“¢ New post: ${title}\n${link}`;         if (S_("DISCORD_BROADCAST_WEBHOOK")) postDiscord(S_("DISCORD_BROADCAST_WEBHOOK"), msg);         if (S_("TG_BOT_TOKEN") && S_("TG_BROADCAST_CHAT_ID")) tgSend(S_("TG_BOT_TOKEN"), S_("TG_BROADCAST_CHAT_ID"), msg);         done.setProperty(key,"1");       });     }catch(err){       postDiscord(S_("DISCORD_OPS_WEBHOOK"), `:warning: rssBroadcast error: ${err.message} (${feedUrl})`);     }   }); }  /* ======= helpers ======= */ function mapRow(h, vals){ const o={}; h.forEach((k,i)=>o[k]=vals[i]); return o; } function hasValue(v){ return !(v===undefined||v===null||String(v).trim()===""); } function safe(v){ return v===undefined||v===null? "" : String(v); } function truncate(s,n){ s=safe(s); return s.length>n? s.slice(0,n-1)+"â€¦" : s; } function fmtTelegram(v){ v=safe(v).trim(); if(!v) return ""; return v.startsWith("@")? v : "@"+v; } function normalizeTelegram(v){ v=safe(v).replace(/^@+/,"").replace(/\s+/g,"").trim(); return v||""; } function textOf(p, name){ const c=p.getChild(name); return c? c.getText(): ""; }  function postDiscord(webhook, content){   if(!webhook) return;   UrlFetchApp.fetch(webhook, {     method:"post",     contentType:"application/json",     payload: JSON.stringify({content}),     muteHttpExceptions:true   }); }  function tgSend(token, chatId, text){   if(!token||!chatId) return;   const url = `https://api.telegram.org/bot${token}/sendMessage`;   UrlFetchApp.fetch(url, {     method:"post",     contentType:"application/json",     payload: JSON.stringify({chat_id: chatId, text, parse_mode:"HTML", disable_web_page_preview:true}),     muteHttpExceptions:true   }); }  /* Ensure Status/Notes/Approved exist */ function ensureOpsColumns(sh, header, need){   const missing = need.filter(n=>!header.includes(n));   if (!missing.length) return;   sh.insertColumnsAfter(header.length, missing.length);   const newHeader = header.concat(missing);   sh.getRange(1,1,1,newHeader.length).setValues([newHeader]);   // Make "Approved" a checkbox if we just created it   const idx = newHeader.indexOf(H.APPROVED)+1;   if (idx>0){     const rule = SpreadsheetApp.newDataValidation().requireCheckbox().build();     sh.getRange(2, idx, sh.getMaxRows()-1, 1).setDataValidation(rule);   } }``

## 3) Add your secrets (Script Properties)

Apps Script editor â†’Â **Project Settings (gear)**Â â†’Â **Script properties**Â â†’ Add these key/value pairs:

- `DISCORD_OPS_WEBHOOK`Â = your #ops-alerts webhook
    
- `DISCORD_BROADCAST_WEBHOOK`Â = (optional) your public/broadcast webhook
    
- `TG_BOT_TOKEN`Â = token from @BotFather
    
- `TG_BROADCAST_CHAT_ID`Â = your channel/group ID (starts withÂ `-100â€¦`)
    
- `TG_GROUP_INVITE_LINK`Â = your private invite link (e.g.,Â `https://t.me/+abcDEFâ€¦`)
    
- `OPS_EMAIL`Â =Â `pimpfiles@proton.me`Â (optional if you also want email)
    

## 4) Add triggers

- **onFormSubmit**Â â†’ From spreadsheet â†’ On form submit
    
- **onEdit**Â is automatic
    
- **rssBroadcast**Â â†’ Time-driven â†’ everyÂ **30 minutes**Â (or hourly)
    

## 5) How to use (fast)

- New submission â†’ shows in sheet and pingsÂ **#ops-alerts**
    
- To approve:Â **tick the Approved checkbox**Â (or useÂ **Vault Ops â†’ Approve selected**)
    
- Script posts an approval line taggingÂ **@username**Â and includes theÂ **invite link**Â in your TG broadcast channel.
    
    - (If you want true DM delivery, make usersÂ `/start`Â your bot first; I can add a â€œchat_id captureâ€ flow next.)
