why is is so slow

###### ChatGPT said:

Short answer: a few usual culprits â€” and we can nuke them fast.

## Likely causes (and fixes)

1. **In-app browser (QR â†’ X/FB/Telegram webview)**  
    Those mini browsers block redirects/popups.  
    **Fix:**Â open in a real browser (Safari/Chrome). Add a line onÂ `join.html`: â€œIf this opened inside an app, tap â€¢â€¢â€¢ â†’ Open in Browser.â€
    
2. **VPN/ProtonVPN routing**  
    Exit nodes sometimes rate-limit Google/Discord.  
    **Fix:**Â toggle VPN off for the test, or pick a different exit (PH/SG/JP).
    
3. **Google Form settings**  
    Required fields or validation nags keep bouncing you to the top.  
    **Fix:**Â in the Form, double-check every question is requiredÂ _once_, and only theÂ **Email**Â field has â€œResponse validation â†’ Email.â€ Nothing else should have validation.
    
4. **Apps Script latency**  
    First run after edit is slow (cold start). UrlFetch to Discord/Telegram adds a second or two.  
    **Fix:**Â itâ€™s normal. After the first run, it heats up. Keep the code lean (we did).
    
5. **Discord webhook throttling**  
    Bursts can queue for a sec.  
    **Fix:**Â one message per submit (weâ€™re doing that), no embeds for now.
    
6. **Telegram bot delivery**  
    If you try true DMs before the userÂ `/start`s the bot, it â€œfails silently.â€  
    **Fix:**Â weâ€™re posting to the broadcast channel with @mentions for now. DM mode needs the user to DM your bot first.
    
7. **Browser cache/stale HTML**  
    OldÂ `gate.html`/`join.html`Â gets cached.  
    **Fix:**Â addÂ `?v=3`Â to the URL while testing, or hard-refresh.

# 1) Apps Script (paste all of this)

**Sheet â†’ Extensions â†’ Apps Script â†’ replace everything with this.**

``/***** VAULT â€” Vetting Pipeline (Discord now, Telegram on approval) *****  * Events used:  *  - onFormSubmit  : every new response -> ping #ops-alerts + email  *  - onOpen        : add â€œVault Opsâ€ menu in the Sheet  *  - onEdit        : if â€œApprovedâ€ is checked -> send Telegram invite + post to #ops-alerts  *  * Script Properties required (Project Settings > Script properties):  *  DISCORD_OPS_WEBHOOK      e.g. https://discord.com/api/webhooks/xxx/yyy  *  OPS_EMAIL                e.g. pimpfiles@proton.me   (optional)  *  TG_BOT_TOKEN             e.g. 123456:ABC...         (optional until you enable approvals)  *  TG_BROADCAST_CHAT_ID     e.g. -1001234567890        (channel or group id, negative for channels)  *  TG_GROUP_INVITE_LINK     e.g. https://t.me/+abcdEFG12345  ***********************************************************************/  const SP = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties(); const CFG = {   discord: SP.getProperty('DISCORD_OPS_WEBHOOK') || '',   opsEmail: SP.getProperty('OPS_EMAIL') || '',   tg: {     token:   SP.getProperty('TG_BOT_TOKEN') || '',     chatId:  SP.getProperty('TG_BROADCAST_CHAT_ID') || '',     invite:  SP.getProperty('TG_GROUP_INVITE_LINK') || ''   },   approvedColName: 'Approved',     // Checkbox column name   timestampColName: 'Approved At', // Will be created if missing };  /* ---------- UTIL ---------- */ function _sheet() { return SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSheet(); } function _headers(sh){   sh = sh || _sheet();   const h = (sh.getRange(1,1,1,sh.getLastColumn()).getValues()[0] || []);   const idx = {};   h.forEach((name,i)=> idx[(name||'').trim()] = i+1);   return { list: h, idx }; } function _now(){ return Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), Session.getScriptTimeZone(), 'yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss'); }  function _postDiscord(content){   if (!CFG.discord) return;   const payload = { content: content.slice(0,1900) }; // keep under limit   UrlFetchApp.fetch(CFG.discord, {     method:'post',     contentType:'application/json',     muteHttpExceptions:true,     payload: JSON.stringify(payload)   }); } function _mail(subject, body){   if (!CFG.opsEmail) return;   MailApp.sendEmail({ to: CFG.opsEmail, subject, body }); } function _tgSend(text){   if (!CFG.tg.token || !CFG.tg.chatId) return;   const url = `https://api.telegram.org/bot${CFG.tg.token}/sendMessage`;   const payload = {     chat_id: CFG.tg.chatId,     text: text,     parse_mode: 'HTML',     disable_web_page_preview: true   };   UrlFetchApp.fetch(url, {     method:'post',     contentType:'application/json',     muteHttpExceptions:true,     payload: JSON.stringify(payload)   }); }  /* ---------- MENU ---------- */ function onOpen(){   SpreadsheetApp.getUi()     .createMenu('Vault Ops')     .addItem('Approve selected', 'approveSelected')     .addToUi();    // Ensure â€œApproved Atâ€ column exists   const sh = _sheet(); const { list, idx } = _headers(sh);   if (!idx[CFG.timestampColName]){     sh.getRange(1, list.length+1).setValue(CFG.timestampColName);   } }  /* ---------- FORM SUBMIT ---------- */ function onFormSubmit(e){   try{     const nv = e && e.namedValues ? e.namedValues : {};     // Build summary     let lines = ['**New Vetting Submission**'];     Object.keys(nv).forEach(k => {       const v = (nv[k] || []).join(', ');       lines.push(`â€¢ **${k}**: ${v}`);     });     const msg = lines.join('\n');      _postDiscord(msg);     _mail('New Vetting Submission', msg);   }catch(err){     _postDiscord(`onFormSubmit error: ${err}`);   } }  /* ---------- ON EDIT: checkbox approval ---------- */ function onEdit(e){   try{     const range = e.range;     const sh = range.getSheet();     const row = range.getRow();     const col = range.getColumn();     if (row === 1) return;      const { idx } = _headers(sh);     const approvedCol = idx[CFG.approvedColName];     if (!approvedCol) return;      // Only act if the changed cell is in â€œApprovedâ€ column     if (col !== approvedCol) return;      const approved = String(range.getValue()).toLowerCase() === 'true';     if (!approved) return;      // Stamp Approved At     const tsCol = idx[CFG.timestampColName] || sh.getLastColumn()+1;     sh.getRange(row, tsCol).setValue(_now());      // Gather row data     const rowVals = sh.getRange(row, 1, 1, sh.getLastColumn()).getValues()[0];     const headers = Object.keys(idx).sort((a,b)=> idx[a]-idx[b]);     const record = {};     headers.forEach(h => { record[h] = rowVals[idx[h]-1]; });      // Compose approval message     const who = record['Alias / Handle'] || record['Full Name'] || 'Applicant';     const email = record['Email'] || '';     const invite = CFG.tg.invite ? `\nTelegram invite: ${CFG.tg.invite}` : '';      const approvedMsgDisc = `âœ… **Approved:** ${who}\n${email ? 'Email: '+email+'\n' : ''}Row #${row}${invite}`;     _postDiscord(approvedMsgDisc);      if (CFG.tg.token && CFG.tg.chatId){       const approvedMsgTG = `âœ… <b>Approved:</b> ${who}${email ? '\nEmail: '+email : ''}${invite ? '\n'+invite : ''}`;       _tgSend(approvedMsgTG);     }    }catch(err){     _postDiscord(`onEdit error: ${err}`);   } }  /* ---------- MENU ACTION ---------- */ function approveSelected(){   const sh = _sheet();   const { idx } = _headers(sh);   const approvedCol = idx[CFG.approvedColName];   if (!approvedCol) {     SpreadsheetApp.getUi().alert(`Missing column: ${CFG.approvedColName}`);     return;   }   const sel = sh.getActiveRange();   const r1 = sel.getRow(), r2 = r1 + sel.getNumRows() - 1;   for (let r = Math.max(2,r1); r <= r2; r++){     sh.getRange(r, approvedCol).setValue(true);   } }``

## **How to auto-write chats & ops notes to Obsidian**

Weâ€™d use a littleÂ **log script**Â that runs each time we push/pull or close the Vault:

1. **Choose your Vault log folder**  
    Example:
    
    `/Users/rican4jesus/Desktop/VaultLogs`
    
2. **Modify VaultPush.command / VaultPull.command / CloseVault.command**  
    Add these lines at the end of each script:
    
    `# Append timestamp + message to today's log in Obsidian vault LOG_DIR="/Users/rican4jesus/Desktop/VaultLogs" TODAY_FILE="$LOG_DIR/$(date +'%Y-%m-%d')-ops-log.md" mkdir -p "$LOG_DIR"  echo "### $(date +'%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')" >> "$TODAY_FILE" echo "$1" >> "$TODAY_FILE"   # Optional arg from script echo "" >> "$TODAY_FILE"  # Open in Obsidian if available open -a "Obsidian" "$TODAY_FILE"`
    
3. **Bonus â€” paste our ChatGPT summaries in there**  
    Every time we finish a session, I can dump aÂ **Ops Summary**Â block that you can paste into the log file.  
    If we want to automate that even more, we can hook anÂ **n8n node**Â that sends our session transcript to your Mac and appends it directly into that file.
    
4. **Result**
    
    - Every pull/push/close writes a time-stamped entry.
        
    - Obsidian opens to todayâ€™s log automatically so you can type extra notes.
        
    - You end up withÂ **one Markdown file per day**Â inside your vault log folder.

ThatÂ **â€œVault not foundâ€**Â error in Obsidian pops when you try to open aÂ `.md`Â file with theÂ `obsidian://`Â URL scheme but the file pathÂ **isnâ€™t inside a registered vault**. Obsidian only knows how to handle files inside a folder youâ€™ve told it is a vault. Right now your script is pointing to:

`/Users/rican4jesus/Desktop/Vault_Ops_Logs/2025-08-21-ops-log.md`

â€¦but Obsidian doesnâ€™t recognizeÂ `Vault_Ops_Logs`Â as part of your vault.

---

âœ…Â **Fix: Make sure the folder is inside your Obsidian vault**

1. Move yourÂ `Vault_Ops_Logs`Â folderÂ **into**Â your Obsidian vault root (e.g.Â `/Users/rican4jesus/Documents/The_Vault/`).
    
    - So it looks like:
        
        `The_Vault/   â”œâ”€â”€ Vault_Ops_Logs/   â”‚     â””â”€â”€ 2025-08-21-ops-log.md`
        
2. Open Obsidian â†’Â `Settings â†’ Files & Links`Â â†’ make sureÂ **â€œDefault location for new notesâ€**Â is pointing insideÂ `The_Vault`.
    

---

âœ…Â **Fix the script to always point to your vault**  
If your vault is calledÂ `The_Vault`, the open command should look like:

`open "obsidian://open?vault=The_Vault&file=Vault_Ops_Logs/2025-08-21-ops-log.md"`

- `vault=The_Vault`Â â†’ must match your actual vault name (case-sensitive).
    
- `file=Vault_Ops_Logs/...`Â â†’ relative path inside the vault.

- That way youâ€™ll never see â€œVault not foundâ€ again.

# 0) Quick glossary

- **Sheet = database.**Â Start with a single Google Sheet now; you can move to Supabase later without changing the UI.
    
- **Apps Script = API.**Â One file gives youÂ `/list`,Â `/geojson`, andÂ `/new`Â endpoints.
    
- **GUI (staff console).**Â Private page in your repo:Â `/staff/console.html`.
    
- **Map.**Â Public pageÂ `/map.html`Â (readâ€‘only; only showsÂ _approved_Â points).
    

---

# 1) Create the Sheet (your DB)

Create a Google Sheet namedÂ **`Vault_DB`**Â with a first sheet namedÂ **`pimps`**Â and these headers in row 1 (exact names):

`id, created_at, status, name, org, country, region, city, lat, lng, tags, tactic, sources, note, language, submitted_by, vetted_by, risk`

- `status`Â =Â `pending`Â |Â `approved`Â |Â `rejected`
    
- `country`Â one of:Â `PH`,Â `PR`,Â `US`Â (you can add more)
    
- `lat/lng`Â are optional; if blank, the map wonâ€™t place a point
    
- `sources`Â = commaâ€‘separated URLs
    
- `tags`Â = commaâ€‘separated (â€œNGO, church, gov, grant, influencerâ€¦â€)
    

Copy the SheetÂ **ID**Â from the URL (the long string betweenÂ `/d/`Â andÂ `/edit`).

---

# 2) Add your API (one Apps Script)

In the Sheet:Â **Extensions â†’ Apps Script**Â â†’ create fileÂ **`Code.gs`**Â and paste:

``/***** VAULT DB API â€” Google Apps Script *****  * Endpoints:  *   GET  ?route=list                 -> JSON rows (all)  *   GET  ?route=geojson&country=PH   -> Points as GeoJSON (status=approved)  *   POST route=new                   -> Add a new record (JSON body)  * Integration: Discord & Telegram alerts on approved/new  ********************************************/  // ==== EDIT THESE ==== const SHEET_NAME = 'pimps'; const SHEET_ID   = 'PASTE_YOUR_SHEET_ID'; const DISCORD_WEBHOOK = 'https://discord.com/api/webhooks/xxx/yyy';  // #ops-alerts const TELEGRAM_BOT_TOKEN = '000000:AA...';  // optional const TELEGRAM_CHAT_ID   = '-1001234567890'; // your channel/supergroup id // ====================  function _sheet() {   return SpreadsheetApp.openById(SHEET_ID).getSheetByName(SHEET_NAME); }  function doGet(e) {   const route = (e.parameter.route || '').toLowerCase();   _addCors();   if (route === 'list') return _json(_list());   if (route === 'geojson') return _json(_geojson(e.parameter.country));   return _json({ok:false, error:'unknown route'}); }  function doPost(e) {   _addCors();   try {     const route = (e.parameter.route || '').toLowerCase();     const body = e.postData && e.postData.contents ? JSON.parse(e.postData.contents) : {};     if (route === 'new') return _json(_create(body));     if (route === 'approve') return _json(_approve(body.id, body.vetted_by || 'ops'));     return _json({ok:false, error:'unknown route'});   } catch (err) {     return _json({ok:false, error:String(err)});   } }  // ===== Core ops =====  function _list() {   const sh = _sheet();   const rows = sh.getDataRange().getValues();   const headers = rows.shift();   return {     ok: true,     rows: rows.map(r => Object.fromEntries(r.map((v,i)=>[headers[i], v])))   }; }  function _create(data) {   const sh = _sheet();   const now = new Date();   const id  = 'pmp_' + now.getTime();   const row = [     id, now, data.status || 'pending',     data.name || '', data.org || '', data.country || '',     data.region || '', data.city || '', Number(data.lat)||'', Number(data.lng)||'',     _csv(data.tags), data.tactic || '', _csv(data.sources),     data.note || '', (data.language||'EN').toUpperCase(),     data.submitted_by || '', '', data.risk || ''   ];   sh.appendRow(row);    // Ping Discord on new row   _discord(`ğŸ§¾ New submission: **${data.name||'N/A'}** (${data.country||'?'})\n${_firstUrl(data.sources)}`);    return {ok:true, id}; }  function _approve(id, vettedBy) {   const sh = _sheet();   const values = sh.getDataRange().getValues();   const headers = values.shift();   const idxStatus = headers.indexOf('status');   const idxId     = headers.indexOf('id');   const idxVetted = headers.indexOf('vetted_by');   let updated = false;   values.forEach((r, i) => {     if (r[idxId] === id) {       sh.getRange(i+2, idxStatus+1).setValue('approved');       sh.getRange(i+2, idxVetted+1).setValue(vettedBy);       updated = true;     }   });   if (updated) {     _discord(`âœ… Approved: ${id}`);     _telegram(`âœ… Approved: ${id}`);   }   return {ok: updated}; }  function _geojson(country) {   const rows = _list().rows.filter(r => r.status === 'approved');   const f = (country ? rows.filter(r=> (r.country||'').toUpperCase() === country.toUpperCase()) : rows)     .filter(r => r.lat && r.lng)     .map(r => ({       type: 'Feature',       properties: {         id: r.id, name: r.name, org: r.org,         country: r.country, city: r.city, tags: r.tags, sources: r.sources       },       geometry: { type: 'Point', coordinates: [Number(r.lng), Number(r.lat)] }     }));   return {type:'FeatureCollection', features: f}; }  // ===== helpers =====  function _csv(x){ return Array.isArray(x) ? x.join(', ') : (x||''); } function _firstUrl(s){ if (!s) return ''; const m=String(s).match(/https?:\/\/\S+/); return m?m[0]:''; } function _json(obj){ return ContentService.createTextOutput(JSON.stringify(obj)).setMimeType(ContentService.MimeType.JSON); } function _addCors(){   const rc = HtmlService.createHtmlOutput('');   rc.addMetaTag('Access-Control-Allow-Origin','*'); } function _discord(msg){   if (!DISCORD_WEBHOOK) return;   try{     UrlFetchApp.fetch(DISCORD_WEBHOOK, {       method:'post',       headers:{'Content-Type':'application/json'},       payload: JSON.stringify({content: msg})     });   }catch(e){} } function _telegram(msg){   if (!TELEGRAM_BOT_TOKEN || !TELEGRAM_CHAT_ID) return;   const url = `https://api.telegram.org/bot${TELEGRAM_BOT_TOKEN}/sendMessage`;   try{     UrlFetchApp.fetch(url, {       method:'post',       payload: { chat_id: TELEGRAM_CHAT_ID, text: msg, parse_mode:'HTML' }     });   }catch(e){} }``

**Deploy it:**

- **Deploy â†’ New deployment â†’ Web app**
    
- Who has access:Â **Anyone**
    
- Copy theÂ **web app URL**Â (looks likeÂ `https://script.google.com/macros/s/XYZ/exec`).
    

Weâ€™ll refer to that asÂ **`API_URL`**Â below.

# 3) Staff Console (private page)

Add this file to your repo asÂ **`/staff/console.html`**Â (link it only from your private ops):

``<!doctype html> <html lang="en"> <head> <meta charset="utf-8" /> <meta name="robots" content="noindex,nofollow" /> <meta name="referrer" content="no-referrer" /> <meta viewport="width=device-width, initial-scale=1" /> <title>Vault Staff Console</title> <style>   body{background:#0b0c10;color:#e8eaf0;font:15px/1.5 system-ui;margin:40px;}   h1{font-size:22px;margin:0 0 12px}   .row{display:flex;gap:18px;flex-wrap:wrap}   .card{background:#13141a;border:1px solid #23242b;border-radius:12px;padding:16px}   input,select,textarea{background:#0f1015;color:#e8eaf0;border:1px solid #2b2c35;border-radius:8px;padding:8px}   table{border-collapse:collapse;width:100%}   th,td{border-bottom:1px solid #1f2027;padding:8px;text-align:left;font-size:13px}   button{background:#3a63ff;border:0;color:#fff;padding:10px 14px;border-radius:10px;cursor:pointer}   .ok{background:#2e9b4d} </style> </head> <body> <h1>Vault Staff Console</h1>  <div class="row">   <div class="card" style="flex:1;min-width:320px">     <h3>Add new record</h3>     <div class="row">       <input id="name" placeholder="Name" />       <input id="org" placeholder="Org" />       <select id="country">         <option value="PH">PH</option>         <option value="PR">PR</option>         <option value="US">US</option>       </select>       <input id="city" placeholder="City" />       <input id="lat" placeholder="Lat" />       <input id="lng" placeholder="Lng" />     </div>     <div class="row">       <input id="tags" placeholder="tags (comma)" style="flex:1" />       <input id="sources" placeholder="sources URLs (comma)" style="flex:1" />     </div>     <textarea id="note" placeholder="note" rows="3" style="width:100%"></textarea>     <div style="margin-top:10px">       <button id="btnNew">Save</button>     </div>     <div id="newMsg" style="margin-top:8px;opacity:.8"></div>   </div>    <div class="card" style="flex:2;min-width:420px">     <h3>Records</h3>     <div class="row">       <select id="filterCountry"><option value="">All</option><option>PH</option><option>PR</option><option>US</option></select>       <select id="filterStatus"><option value="">Any status</option><option>pending</option><option>approved</option></select>       <button class="ok" id="btnRefresh">Refresh</button>     </div>     <table id="grid"><thead>       <tr><th>id</th><th>name</th><th>org</th><th>country</th><th>city</th><th>status</th><th>approve</th></tr>     </thead><tbody></tbody></table>   </div> </div>  <script> const API = 'PASTE_API_URL_HERE';  async function api(route, payload){   const opt = payload ? {method:'POST', headers:{'Content-Type':'application/json'}, body:JSON.stringify(payload)} : {};   const url = payload ? `${API}?route=${route}` : `${API}?route=${route}`;   const r = await fetch(url, opt); return r.json(); }  async function refresh(){   const fc = document.getElementById('filterCountry').value;   const fs = document.getElementById('filterStatus').value;   const data = await api('list');   const rows = data.rows.filter(r => (!fc || r.country===fc) && (!fs || r.status===fs));   const tb = document.querySelector('#grid tbody'); tb.innerHTML='';   rows.forEach(r=>{     const tr = document.createElement('tr');     tr.innerHTML = `<td>${r.id}</td><td>${r.name||''}</td><td>${r.org||''}</td><td>${r.country||''}</td><td>${r.city||''}</td><td>${r.status||''}</td>                     <td>${r.status==='approved' ? 'â€”' : `<button data-id="${r.id}" class="ok">Approve</button>`}</td>`;     tb.appendChild(tr);   }); } document.getElementById('btnRefresh').onclick = refresh; document.getElementById('grid').onclick = async (e)=>{   if (e.target.tagName==='BUTTON' && e.target.dataset.id){     await api('approve', {id:e.target.dataset.id, vetted_by:'ops'});     refresh();   } }; document.getElementById('btnNew').onclick = async ()=>{   const payload = {     name: val('name'), org: val('org'), country: val('country'),     city: val('city'), lat: val('lat'), lng: val('lng'),     tags: val('tags'), sources: val('sources'), note: val('note'),     status:'pending', submitted_by:'staff', language:'EN'   };   const out = await api('new', payload);   document.getElementById('newMsg').textContent = out.ok ? `Saved: ${out.id}` : (out.error||'Error');   refresh(); }; function val(id){ return document.getElementById(id).value.trim(); } refresh(); </script> </body> </html>``

> This console lets youÂ **add entries**, filter, andÂ **Approve**. Approving triggersÂ **Discord**Â andÂ **Telegram**Â pings automatically.

---

# 4) Public map (readâ€‘only)

AddÂ **`/map.html`**:

``<!doctype html> <html lang="en"> <head> <meta charset="utf-8" /> <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1"> <title>Poverty Pimp Heatmap</title> <link rel="stylesheet" href="https://unpkg.com/leaflet@1.9.4/dist/leaflet.css"> <script src="https://unpkg.com/leaflet@1.9.4/dist/leaflet.js"></script> <style>   html,body,#map{height:100%;margin:0}   .ctl{position:fixed;top:12px;left:12px;background:#0f1015;color:#e8eaf0;padding:8px 10px;border-radius:10px;box-shadow:0 2px 12px rgba(0,0,0,.35)}   select{background:#0f1015;color:#e8eaf0;border:1px solid #2b2c35;border-radius:8px;padding:6px} </style> </head> <body> <div class="ctl">Country:   <select id="cc">     <option value="">All</option><option>PH</option><option>PR</option><option>US</option>   </select> </div> <div id="map"></div> <script> const API = 'PASTE_API_URL_HERE';  const map = L.map('map').setView([14.5995,120.9842], 4); L.tileLayer('https://{s}.tile.openstreetmap.org/{z}/{x}/{y}.png',{maxZoom:19}).addTo(map); let layer;  async function draw(){   const cc = document.getElementById('cc').value;   const url = cc ? `${API}?route=geojson&country=${cc}` : `${API}?route=geojson`;   const data = await fetch(url).then(r=>r.json());   if (layer){ layer.remove(); }   layer = L.geoJSON(data, {     onEachFeature: (f, m) => m.bindPopup(`<b>${f.properties.name||''}</b><br>${f.properties.org||''}<br>${f.properties.city||''}, ${f.properties.country||''}<br><a target=_blank href="${firstUrl(f.properties.sources)}">source</a>`),     pointToLayer: (f, latlng)=> L.circleMarker(latlng,{radius:6, color:'#6a8dff', fillColor:'#6a8dff', fillOpacity:.9 })   }).addTo(map);   if (layer.getLayers().length){ map.fitBounds(layer.getBounds(), {padding:[30,30]}); } } function firstUrl(s){ const m=String(s||'').match(/https?:\/\/\S+/); return m?m[0]:'#'; } document.getElementById('cc').onchange = draw; draw(); </script> </body> </html>``

> Map showsÂ **onlyÂ `approved`**Â entries and autoâ€‘zooms to the data.

# 1) Drop-in â€œfinalâ€ buttons (fixed Obsidian path)

These replace your existing buttons. They willÂ **auto-create the log**,Â **launch Obsidian**, andÂ **open the log**Â inside the right vaultÂ **without errors**.

### ğŸ”µÂ `OpenVault.command`

`#!/bin/zsh set -euo pipefail  # === CONFIG === VAULT_DIR="$HOME/Documents/PovertyPimpsVault"                # your Obsidian vault root LOG_DIR="$VAULT_DIR/Vault_Ops_Logs" TODAY="$(date +%Y-%m-%d)" STAMP="$(date +%H_%M_%S)" LOG_NAME="VaultOps_Shift_Log_${TODAY}_${STAMP}.md" LOG_PATH="${LOG_DIR}/${LOG_NAME}"  # ensure folders mkdir -p "$LOG_DIR"  # seed new shift log cat > "$LOG_PATH" <<'MD' # VaultOps Shift Log â€” {{TODAY}} {{STAMP}}  **Status:** â±ï¸ Shift started   **Ops:** TruthBot Zero  ## Links - Chat log seed: (paste todayâ€™s chat URL here)  ## Plan (quick bullets) - [ ] QR â†’ join â†’ Discord check - [ ] gate.html passcode + form reveal - [ ] Form submit â†’ Discord #ops-alerts + email - [ ] Beta intake (ES/TL/EN) smoke test  ## Notes -  MD  # stamp values into template LC_ALL=C sed -i '' "s/{{TODAY}}/${TODAY}/g;s/{{STAMP}}/${STAMP}/g" "$LOG_PATH"  # launch Obsidian on the VAULT, then open the file open -a "Obsidian" "$VAULT_DIR" sleep 2  # Try deep-link (works even without Advanced URI plugin) # Obsidian accepts file path URLs; basic escaping: url_path="$(python3 - <<PY import urllib.parse,sys p=sys.argv[1] print('obsidian://open?path='+urllib.parse.quote(p)) PY "$LOG_PATH")"  open "$url_path"  echo "âœ… Opened: $LOG_PATH"`

### ğŸ”´Â `CloseVault.command`

`#!/bin/zsh set -euo pipefail  VAULT_DIR="$HOME/Documents/PovertyPimpsVault" LOG_DIR="$VAULT_DIR/Vault_Ops_Logs"  # find most recent shift log from today LAST_LOG="$(ls -t "$LOG_DIR"/VaultOps_Shift_Log_*.md 2>/dev/null | head -n 1 || true)" if [[ -z "${LAST_LOG}" ]]; then   echo "âš ï¸ No shift log found in $LOG_DIR"   exit 0 fi  ENDSTAMP="$(date +%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S)" cat >> "$LAST_LOG" <<MD  ---  ### Shift closed **Time:** ${ENDSTAMP}   **Summary:**   - (fill before closing)  MD  # Open in Obsidian so you can write the last 2 bullet points and close. open -a "Obsidian" "$VAULT_DIR" sleep 2 url_path="$(python3 - <<PY import urllib.parse,sys p=sys.argv[1] print('obsidian://open?path='+urllib.parse.quote(p)) PY "$LAST_LOG")" open "$url_path"  echo "ğŸ”’ Closed: $LAST_LOG"`

**Install (one-time):**

1. Open Terminal and paste:
    
    `cat > ~/Desktop/OpenVault.command <<'EOF' # (paste the WHOLE OpenVault.command script here) EOF cat > ~/Desktop/CloseVault.command <<'EOF' # (paste the WHOLE CloseVault.command script here) EOF chmod +x ~/Desktop/OpenVault.command ~/Desktop/CloseVault.command`
    
2. Double-clickÂ **OpenVault.command**Â â†’ youâ€™ll see todayâ€™s log open in Obsidian.
    
3. When ending the shift, double-clickÂ **CloseVault.command**Â â†’ the log is stamped and opened for your last two bullets.
    

> If Obsidian prompts â€œVault not foundâ€, make sure your vault is at:  
> `/Users/rican4jesus/Documents/PovertyPimpsVault`  
> (Thatâ€™s what the buttons are pointed at now.)

### Where to paste code

Form editor â†’ â‹®Â **Script editor**Â (Apps Script) â†’ create/replaceÂ `Code.gs`Â with this:

``/***** VAULT â€” Vetting Pipeline (stable) *****/  // EDIT THESE TWO: const DISCORD_WEBHOOK = "PASTE_YOUR_ops-alerts_WEBHOOK"; const OPS_EMAIL       = "pimpfiles@proton.me";  /** On form submit: send Discord alert + Ops email */ function onFormSubmit(e) {   try {     const nv = e.namedValues || {};     const row = Object.fromEntries(Object.entries(nv).map(([k,v])=>[k, Array.isArray(v)?v.join(", ").trim():String(v||"").trim()]));      const summary =       `**New Vetting Request**\n` +       `â€¢ **Email:** ${row["Email"] || "N/A"}\n` +       `â€¢ **Full Name:** ${row["Full Name"] || "N/A"}\n` +       `â€¢ **Alias / Handle:** ${row["Alias / Handle"] || "N/A"}\n` +       `â€¢ **Role:** ${row["Role"] || "N/A"}\n` +       `â€¢ **Why join:** ${row["What motivated you to join The Vault? (Paragraph)"] || "N/A"}\n` +       `â€¢ **Contribute:** ${row["What can you contribute?"] || "N/A"}\n` +       `â€¢ **Links:** ${row["Share 1â€“3 links that show your signal (thread/posts)"] || "N/A"}\n` +       `â€¢ **Telegram/Signal:** ${row["Telegram/Signal handle"] || "N/A"}\n` +       `â€¢ **Country:** ${row["Country"] || "N/A"}`;      // Discord     UrlFetchApp.fetch(DISCORD_WEBHOOK, {       method: "post",       contentType: "application/json",       payload: JSON.stringify({ content: summary.slice(0, 1800) }) // guard size     });      // Email     MailApp.sendEmail({       to: OPS_EMAIL,       subject: "New Vault Vetting Request",       body: summary     });    } catch (err) {     console.error("onFormSubmit error:", err);   } }  /** Add Sheet menu to approve rows later (placeholder for Telegram auto-invite) */ function onOpen() {   const ui = SpreadsheetApp.getUi();   ui.createMenu("Vault Ops")     .addItem("Approve selected (stub)", "approveSelected")     .addToUi(); } function approveSelected() {   SpreadsheetApp.getActive().toast("Approve flow stub â€“ ready for Telegram wiring."); }  /** Helper for manual backfill (call from Run menu) */ function triageBackfillAll() {   const sh = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSheet();   const data = sh.getDataRange().getValues();   const header = data.shift();   const toObj = (row)=> header.reduce((o, k, i)=> (o[k]=row[i], o), {});   data.forEach(row => onFormSubmit({ namedValues: toObj(row) })); }``

Leave null to use the active sheet */ const SHEET_NAME = null; /** === MAIN ON-EDIT HOOK (install a trigger: From spreadsheet â†’ On edit) === */ function onEditEvidence(e) { try { const sh = SHEET_NAME ? e.source.getSheetByName(SHEET_NAME) : e.range.getSheet(); if (!sh) return; const header = sh.getRange(1, 1, 1, sh.getLastColumn()).getValues()[0]; // Resolve columns by header text (case-insensitive regex) const col = { triage: findHeader(header, /triage status/i), reviewed:findHeader(header, /reviewed date/i), severity:findHeader(header, /severity/i), who: findHeader(header, /name of individual\/organization/i), links: findHeader(header, /links to evidence/i), desc: findHeader(header, /brief description/i), notes: findHeader(header, /notes/i) }; const r = e.range.getRow(); const c = e.range.getColumn(); if (r === 1) return; // ignore header edits // Stamp Reviewed Date when TRIAGE changes if (c === col.triage && col.reviewed > 0) { sh.getRange(r, col.reviewed).setValue(new Date()); } // Suggest Severity on edits to links/description/triage if ([col.links, col.desc, col.triage].includes(c) && col.severity > 0) { const links = getCell(sh, r, col.links); const desc = getCell(sh, r, col.desc); sh.getRange(r, col.severity).setValue(suggestSeverity(`${links} ${desc}`)); } // Normalize link when Links column edited if (c === col.links && col.links > 0) { const v = String(getCell(sh, r, col.links) || "").trim(); if (v && !/^https?:\/\//i.test(v)) sh.getRange(r, col.links).setValue("https://" + v); } // Handle explicit Drop status (no syntax errors) if (col.triage > 0) { const status = String(getCell(sh, r, col.triage) || "").trim(); if (status === "Drop") { // Optional: annotate notes, set severity low if (col.notes > 0) sh.getRange(r, col.notes).setNote("Marked Drop by Ops"); if (col.severity > 0) sh.getRange(r, col.severity).setValue("Low"); } } // If severity is HIGH, ping Discord + email Ops (once per edit) if (col.severity > 0) { const sev = String(getCell(sh, r, col.severity) || ""); if (sev.toLowerCase() === "high") { const who = col.who > 0 ? String(getCell(sh, r, col.who) || "") : ""; const links = col.links > 0 ? String(getCell(sh, r, col.links) || "") : ""; const desc = col.desc > 0 ? String(getCell(sh, r, col.desc) || "") : ""; safePingDiscord(`ğŸš¨ **High Severity Evidence**` **Name/Org:** ${who} **Links:** ${links} **Notes:** ${desc ? (desc.length>500 ? desc.slice(0,500)+'â€¦' : desc) : '(none)'} (Row ${r})`);` safeMail(OPS_EMAIL, "[VAULT] High Severity Evidence", htmlPre( High Severity Evidence (Row ${r}) Name/Org: ${who} Links: ${links} Notes: ${desc} `));` } } } catch (err) { Logger.log("onEditEvidence error: " + err); } } /** === UTILITIES === */ function findHeader(headerRow, regex) { for (var i = 0; i < headerRow.length; i++) { var h = String(headerRow[i] || ""); if (regex.test(h)) return i + 1; // 1-based col index } return -1; } function getCell(sh, row, col) { return (col > 0) ? sh.getRange(row, col).getValue() : ""; } function suggestSeverity(text) { const t = String(text || "").toLowerCase(); const high = /(fraud|money laundering|kickback|ghost|scam|theft|embezzl|bribe|pork)/; const med = /(nepotism|conflict|misuse|misreport|coi|irregular)/; if (high.test(t)) return "High"; if (med.test(t)) return "Medium"; return "Low"; } function safePingDiscord(content) { try { if (!DISCORD_WEBHOOK || DISCORD_WEBHOOK.indexOf("https://") !== 0) return; UrlFetchApp.fetch(DISCORD_WEBHOOK, { method: "post", contentType: "application/json", payload: JSON.stringify({ username: "Vault Evidence Bot", content }) }); } catch (e) { Logger.log("Discord error: " + e); } } function safeMail(to, subject, htmlBody) { try { if (!to) return; MailApp.sendEmail({ to, subject, htmlBody }); } catch (e) { Logger.log("Mail error: " + e); } } function htmlPre(text) { const esc = String(text).replace(/[&<>]/g, m => ({'&':'&amp;','<':'&lt;','>':'&gt;'}[m])); return "<pre style='font-family:monospace'>" + esc + "</pre>"; } /** === BULK BACKFILL (menu action) === */ function triageBackfillAll() { const sh = SHEET_NAME ? SpreadsheetApp.getActive().getSheetByName(SHEET_NAME) : SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSheet(); const header = sh.getRange(1, 1, 1, sh.getLastColumn()).getValues()[0]; const col = { triage: findHeader(header, /triage status/i), reviewed:findHeader(header, /reviewed date/i), severity:findHeader(header, /severity/i), links: findHeader(header, /links to evidence/i), desc: findHeader(header, /brief description/i) }; const last = sh.getLastRow(); for (var r = 2; r <= last; r++) { try { const triage = String(getCell(sh, r, col.triage) || ""); const reviewed = getCell(sh, r, col.reviewed); if (triage && triage.toLowerCase() !== "new" && !reviewed && col.reviewed > 0) { sh.getRange(r, col.reviewed).setValue(new Date()); } if (col.severity > 0) { const links = String(getCell(sh, r, col.links) || ""); const desc = String(getCell(sh, r, col.desc) || ""); sh.getRange(r, col.severity).setValue(suggestSeverity(`${links} ${desc}`)); } } catch (_) {} } } /** Add menu for backfill */ function onOpen() { SpreadsheetApp.getUi() .createMenu("Vault Ops") .addItem("Backfill Triage/Severity", "triageBackfillAll") .addToUi(); }

function buildOpsDashboard() { const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet(); const dataSh = ss.getSheetByName('Form Responses 1'); if (!dataSh) throw new Error('Need a tab called "Form Responses 1".'); // Create / reset Ops Dashboard let ops = ss.getSheetByName('Ops Dashboard'); if (!ops) { ops = ss.insertSheet('Ops Dashboard'); } else { ops.clear(); } // Identify Status column const headers = dataSh.getRange(1, 1, 1, dataSh.getLastColumn()).getValues()[0]; const statusIdx = headers.findIndex(h => String(h).trim().toLowerCase() === 'status'); if (statusIdx < 0) throw new Error('Add a "Status" header in Form Responses 1 first.'); const statusCol = "AD"; // Hardcoded, since your Status column is AD const src = `'Form Responses 1'`; // Title ops.getRange('A1').setValue('ğŸ“Š Ops Dashboard').setFontWeight("bold"); // KPI labels const labels = ['Total Submissions','Approved','Review','Rejected','Pending (blank/Unapproved)']; ops.getRange('A3:A7').setValues(labels.map(l => [l])); // KPI formulas ops.getRange('B3').setFormula(`=COUNTA(${src}!A2:A)`); ops.getRange('B4').setFormula(`=COUNTIF(FILTER(${src}!${statusCol}2:${statusCol},LEN(${src}!A2:A)),"Approved âœ…")`); ops.getRange('B5').setFormula(`=COUNTIF(FILTER(${src}!${statusCol}2:${statusCol},LEN(${src}!A2:A)),"REVIEW*")`); ops.getRange('B6').setFormula(`=COUNTIF(FILTER(${src}!${statusCol}2:${statusCol},LEN(${src}!A2:A)),"REJECT*")`); ops.getRange('B7').setFormula(`=B3-B4-B5-B6`); // Section tables ops.getRange('A9').setValue('âœ… Approved').setFontWeight("bold"); ops.getRange('A10').setFormula(`=IFERROR(FILTER(${src}!A2:ZZ,${src}!${statusCol}2:${statusCol}="Approved âœ…"),"")`); ops.getRange('A21').setValue('ğŸŸ£ Review').setFontWeight("bold"); ops.getRange('A22').setFormula(`=IFERROR(FILTER(${src}!A2:ZZ,REGEXMATCH(${src}!${statusCol}2:${statusCol},"^REVIEW")),"")`); ops.getRange('A33').setValue('â›” Rejected').setFontWeight("bold"); ops.getRange('A34').setFormula(`=IFERROR(FILTER(${src}!A2:ZZ,REGEXMATCH(${src}!${statusCol}2:${statusCol},"^REJECT")),"")`); ops.getRange('A45').setValue('â³ Pending').setFontWeight("bold"); ops.getRange('A46').setFormula(`=IFERROR(FILTER(${src}!A2:ZZ,(LEN(${src}!${statusCol}2:${statusCol})=0)*(LEN(${src}!A2:A)>0) + (${src}!${statusCol}2:${statusCol}="Unapproved â›”")),"")`); ops.autoResizeColumns(1, 5); } /** Sync Status when the Approved checkbox is toggled */ function onEdit(e) { try { const sh = e.range.getSheet(); if (!sh || sh.getName() !== 'Form Responses 1') return; // only on the responses sheet const row = e.range.getRow(); if (row < 2) return; // ignore header row // Find column indexes by header names (robust to column moves) const headers = sh.getRange(1, 1, 1, sh.getLastColumn()).getValues()[0].map(h => String(h).trim()); # 2) Google Sheets â€”Â **one**Â Code.gs for both Vetting + Evidence Drop

Paste thisÂ **entire**Â script intoÂ **Extensions â†’ Apps Script**Â of each Sheet (Vetting sheet and Evidence sheet). It is header-driven, so it adapts to your columns. Then set the triggers I list right after.

**Fill these two (Discord + email).**  
If youâ€™ll use Telegram later, fill the token/chat values and the approval â€œonEditâ€ will DM the invite.

``/***** VAULT â€” Ops Automation (Vetting + Evidence) *****  * - Vetting onSubmit â†’ Discord + email (safe length)  * - Evidence onEdit â†’ triage stamps, severity guess, link normalize, HIGH ping  * - Approve checkbox â†’ sets Status and (optional) Telegram invite  * - Menu: Build Ops Dashboard + Backfill Approvedâ†’Status  ********************************************************/  /** ===== CONFIG â€” EDIT THESE ===== */ const DISCORD_WEBHOOK = "PASTE_YOUR_OPS_ALERTS_WEBHOOK";   // e.g. https://discord.com/api/webhooks/xxx/yyy const OPS_EMAIL       = "pimpfiles@proton.me";  // Optional Telegram (sends invite only when approved == TRUE) const TELEGRAM_BOT_TOKEN = "";     // e.g. 123456:ABC... const TELEGRAM_CHAT_ID   = "";     // your target chat/user id const TELEGRAM_INVITE    = "https://t.me/+YOUR_INVITE"; // your private invite link  /** ====== VETTING: on form submit (From spreadsheet â†’ On form submit) ====== */ function onFormSubmit(e) {   try {     const sh = e.range.getSheet();     const headers = sh.getRange(1,1,1,sh.getLastColumn()).getValues()[0];     const rowVals = sh.getRange(e.range.getRow(), 1, 1, headers.length).getValues()[0];      const obj = {};     headers.forEach((h,i)=> obj[String(h).trim()] = rowVals[i]);      // Common likely fields. Adjust names to your headers if different.     const name   = obj["Full Name"] || obj["Name"] || "";     const alias  = obj["Alias / Handle"] || obj["Alias"] || "";     const email  = obj["Email"] || "";     const role   = obj["Role"] || "";     const links  = obj["Share 1â€“3 links that show your signal (thread, receipts, analysis)"] || obj["Links"] || "";     const oath   = obj["I agree to follow the Vault Oath"] || obj["Oath"] || "";     const when   = obj["Timestamp"] || new Date();      const msg = `ğŸ“ **New Vetting Request** **Name:** ${name} **Alias:** ${alias} **Role:** ${role} **Email:** ${email} **Links:** ${links} **Oath:** ${oath} **When:** ${when}`;      safeDiscord(msg);     safeMail(OPS_EMAIL, "[VAULT] New Vetting Request", htmlPre(msg));   } catch (err) {     Logger.log("onFormSubmit error: "+err);   } }  /** ====== EVIDENCE: on edit (From spreadsheet â†’ On edit) ======  * Header driven: looks for columns by regex names, works even if columns move.  */ function onEditEvidence(e) {   try {     const sh = e.range.getSheet();     if (!sh) return;      const header = sh.getRange(1,1,1,sh.getLastColumn()).getValues()[0];      const col = {       triage:   findHeader(header, /triage status/i),       reviewed: findHeader(header, /reviewed date/i),       severity: findHeader(header, /severity/i),       who:      findHeader(header, /name of individual\/?organization/i),       links:    findHeader(header, /links to evidence/i),       desc:     findHeader(header, /brief description/i),       notes:    findHeader(header, /notes/i)     };      const r = e.range.getRow(), c = e.range.getColumn();     if (r === 1) return;      // Stamp Reviewed Date when TRIAGE changes     if (c === col.triage && col.reviewed > 0) {       sh.getRange(r, col.reviewed).setValue(new Date());     }      // Suggest Severity     if ([col.links, col.desc, col.triage].includes(c) && col.severity > 0) {       const links = getCell(sh, r, col.links);       const desc  = getCell(sh, r, col.desc);       sh.getRange(r, col.severity).setValue(suggestSeverity(`${links} ${desc}`));     }      // Normalize link     if (c === col.links && col.links > 0) {       const v = String(getCell(sh, r, col.links) || "").trim();       if (v && !/^https?:\/\//i.test(v)) sh.getRange(r, col.links).setValue("https://" + v);     }      // Handle explicit Drop safely     if (col.triage > 0) {       const status = String(getCell(sh, r, col.triage) || "").trim();       if (status === "Drop") {         if (col.notes > 0)    sh.getRange(r, col.notes).setNote("Marked Drop by Ops");         if (col.severity > 0) sh.getRange(r, col.severity).setValue("Low");       }     }      // If severity is HIGH, ping Discord + email (truncate body)     if (col.severity > 0) {       const sev = String(getCell(sh, r, col.severity) || "");       if (sev.toLowerCase() === "high") {         const who   = col.who   > 0 ? String(getCell(sh, r, col.who)   || "") : "";         const links = col.links > 0 ? String(getCell(sh, r, col.links) || "") : "";         const desc  = col.desc  > 0 ? String(getCell(sh, r, col.desc)  || "") : "";          const short = desc ? (String(desc).length > 500 ? String(desc).slice(0,500)+"â€¦" : desc) : "(none)";          const msg = `ğŸš¨ **High Severity Evidence** **Name/Org:** ${who} **Links:** ${links} **Notes:** ${short} (Row ${r})`;          safeDiscord(msg);         safeMail(OPS_EMAIL, "[VAULT] High Severity Evidence", htmlPre(msg));       }     }   } catch (err) {     Logger.log("onEditEvidence error: "+err);   } }  /** ====== APPROVALS: toggle checkbox â†’ Status + (optional) Telegram DM ====== */ function onEdit(e) {   try {     const sh = e.range.getSheet();     if (!sh || sh.getName() !== 'Form Responses 1') return;     const row = e.range.getRow();     if (row < 2) return;      const headers = sh.getRange(1,1,1,sh.getLastColumn()).getValues()[0].map(h=>String(h).trim());     const approvedCol = headers.findIndex(h => h.toLowerCase() === 'approved') + 1;     const statusCol   = headers.findIndex(h => h.toLowerCase() === 'status') + 1;     if (!approvedCol || !statusCol) return;      if (e.range.getColumn() !== approvedCol) return;      const checked = e.value === 'TRUE';     const newStatus = checked ? 'Approved âœ…' : 'Unapproved â›”';     sh.getRange(row, statusCol).setValue(newStatus);      // Optional: Telegram DM on approval     if (checked && TELEGRAM_BOT_TOKEN && TELEGRAM_CHAT_ID && TELEGRAM_INVITE) {       const vals = sh.getRange(row,1,1,headers.length).getValues()[0];       const obj = {}; headers.forEach((h,i)=> obj[h]=vals[i]);       const alias = obj['Alias / Handle'] || obj['Alias'] || '';       const text = `âœ… Approved: ${alias}\nHere is your secure invite: ${TELEGRAM_INVITE}\n(Do not share.)`;       safeTelegram(text);     }   } catch (err) {     Logger.log('onEdit (approval) error: '+err);   } }  /** ====== MENU: dashboard + backfills ====== */ function onOpen() {   SpreadsheetApp.getUi()     .createMenu("Vault Ops")     .addItem("Build Ops Dashboard", "buildOpsDashboard")     .addItem("Backfill Approvedâ†’Status", "backfillApprovedToStatus")     .addToUi(); }  function buildOpsDashboard() {   const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();   const dataSh = ss.getSheetByName('Form Responses 1');   if (!dataSh) throw new Error('Need a tab called "Form Responses 1".');    let ops = ss.getSheetByName('Ops Dashboard');   ops ? ops.clear() : ops = ss.insertSheet('Ops Dashboard');    const headers = dataSh.getRange(1,1,1,dataSh.getLastColumn()).getValues()[0].map(h=>String(h));   const statusIdx = headers.findIndex(h => h.trim().toLowerCase() === 'status');   if (statusIdx < 0) throw new Error('Add a "Status" header in Form Responses 1 first.');    const src = `'Form Responses 1'`;   const statusColLetter = columnToLetter(statusIdx+1);    ops.getRange('A1').setValue('ğŸ“Š Ops Dashboard').setFontWeight("bold");   const labels = ['Total Submissions','Approved','Review','Rejected','Pending (blank/Unapproved)'];   ops.getRange('A3:A7').setValues(labels.map(l => [l]));    ops.getRange('B3').setFormula(`=COUNTA(${src}!A2:A)`);   ops.getRange('B4').setFormula(`=COUNTIF(FILTER(${src}!${statusColLetter}2:${statusColLetter},LEN(${src}!A2:A)),"Approved âœ…")`);   ops.getRange('B5').setFormula(`=COUNTIF(FILTER(${src}!${statusColLetter}2:${statusColLetter},LEN(${src}!A2:A)),"REVIEW*")`);   ops.getRange('B6').setFormula(`=COUNTIF(FILTER(${src}!${statusColLetter}2:${statusColLetter},LEN(${src}!A2:A)),"REJECT*")`);   ops.getRange('B7').setFormula(`=B3-B4-B5-B6`);    ops.getRange('A9').setValue('âœ… Approved').setFontWeight("bold");   ops.getRange('A10').setFormula(`=IFERROR(FILTER(${src}!A2:ZZ,${src}!${statusColLetter}2:${statusColLetter}="Approved âœ…"),"")`);    ops.getRange('A21').setValue('ğŸŸ£ Review').setFontWeight("bold");   ops.getRange('A22').setFormula(`=IFERROR(FILTER(${src}!A2:ZZ,REGEXMATCH(${src}!${statusColLetter}2:${statusColLetter},"^REVIEW")),"")`);    ops.getRange('A33').setValue('â›” Rejected').setFontWeight("bold");   ops.getRange('A34').setFormula(`=IFERROR(FILTER(${src}!A2:ZZ,REGEXMATCH(${src}!${statusColLetter}2:${statusColLetter},"^REJECT")),"")`);    ops.getRange('A45').setValue('â³ Pending').setFontWeight("bold");   ops.getRange('A46').setFormula(`=IFERROR(FILTER(${src}!A2:ZZ,(LEN(${src}!${statusColLetter}2:${statusColLetter})=0)*(LEN(${src}!A2:A)>0) + (${src}!${statusColLetter}2:${statusColLetter}="Unapproved â›”")),"")`);    ops.autoResizeColumns(1, 8); }  function backfillApprovedToStatus() {   const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActive();   const sh = ss.getSheetByName('Form Responses 1');   if (!sh) throw new Error('Missing "Form Responses 1" sheet.');    const lastRow = sh.getLastRow();   if (lastRow < 2) return;    const headers = sh.getRange(1,1,1,sh.getLastColumn()).getValues()[0].map(h => String(h).trim());   const approvedCol = headers.findIndex(h => h.toLowerCase()==='approved') + 1;   const statusCol   = headers.findIndex(h => h.toLowerCase()==='status') + 1;   if (!approvedCol || !statusCol) throw new Error('Need "Approved" and "Status" headers in row 1.');    const approvedVals = sh.getRange(2, approvedCol, lastRow-1, 1).getValues();   const out = approvedVals.map(r => (r[0] === true ? ['Approved âœ…'] : ['Unapproved â›”']));   sh.getRange(2, statusCol, lastRow-1, 1).setValues(out); }  /** ====== shared utils ====== */ function findHeader(headerRow, regex){   for (let i=0;i<headerRow.length;i++){     const h = String(headerRow[i]||"");     if (regex.test(h)) return i+1;   }   return -1; } function getCell(sh, row, col){ return (col>0) ? sh.getRange(row,col).getValue() : ""; }  function suggestSeverity(text){   const t = String(text||"").toLowerCase();   const high = /(fraud|money laundering|kickback|ghost|scam|theft|embezzl|bribe|pork)/;   const med  = /(nepotism|conflict|misuse|misreport|coi|irregular)/;   if (high.test(t)) return "High";   if (med.test(t))  return "Medium";   return "Low"; }  function safeDiscord(content){   try{     if (!DISCORD_WEBHOOK || DISCORD_WEBHOOK.indexOf("https://")!==0) return;     const body = JSON.stringify({ username:"Vault Ops Bot", content: String(content).slice(0,1900) });     UrlFetchApp.fetch(DISCORD_WEBHOOK, { method:"post", contentType:"application/json", payload: body });   }catch(e){ Logger.log("Discord error: "+e); } } function safeMail(to, subject, htmlBody){   try{ if(to) MailApp.sendEmail({ to, subject, htmlBody }); }catch(e){ Logger.log("Mail error: "+e); } } function htmlPre(text){   const esc = String(text).replace(/[&<>]/g, m=>({'&':'&amp;','<':'&lt;','>':'&gt;'}[m]));   return "<pre style='font-family:monospace;white-space:pre-wrap'>"+esc+"</pre>"; } function columnToLetter(c){   let s=""; while(c>0){ let m=(c-1)%26; s=String.fromCharCode(65+m)+s; c=(c-m-1)/26; } return s; } function safeTelegram(text){   try{     if(!TELEGRAM_BOT_TOKEN || !TELEGRAM_CHAT_ID) return;     const url = `https://api.telegram.org/bot${TELEGRAM_BOT_TOKEN}/sendMessage`;     const payload = { chat_id: TELEGRAM_CHAT_ID, text: text, disable_web_page_preview: true };     UrlFetchApp.fetch(url, { method:"post", contentType:"application/json", payload: JSON.stringify(payload) });   }catch(e){ Logger.log("Telegram error: "+e); } }``

### Triggers to set (once per sheet)

- **Vetting sheet**:
    
    - Triggers â†’Â **+ Add Trigger**Â â†’Â `onFormSubmit`Â â†’ Event:Â _From spreadsheet_Â /Â _On form submit_.
        
    - Triggers â†’Â **+ Add Trigger**Â â†’Â `onEdit`Â â†’ Event:Â _From spreadsheet_Â /Â _On edit_.
        
- **Evidence sheet**:
    
    - Triggers â†’Â **+ Add Trigger**Â â†’Â `onEditEvidence`Â â†’ Event:Â _From spreadsheet_Â /Â _On edit_.
        
- (Optional) RunÂ **Vault Ops â†’ Build Ops Dashboard**Â once to generate the KPI page.
